# Overview | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/#id-1.-proxyman)

1\. Proxyman


---------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman is a high-performance macOS app that enables developers to view HTTP/HTTPS requests from apps and domains, including iOS devices, iOS Simulators, and Android devices.

![Proxyman dashboard for macOS 26](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FUc6cygtl1lgELnAz8pXy%252Fnew_dashboard_macOS_26.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5827a834-698f-40ce-a550-5cbed8f36da8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ac6fb3e&sv=2)

Proxyman Dashboard for macOS 26

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/#id-2.-features)

2\. Features

*   ✅ Intercept HTTP/HTTPS (SSL) requests from your MacBook, iOS Simulators, iOS devices, and Android devices 📱.
    
*   Built for Apple Silicon Chip and macOS 26 Tahoe
    
*   ✅ 100% written by Apple Swift NIO for high-performance
    
*   🦋 Modern and intuitive UI.
    
*   🍸 Liquid Glass UI for macOS 26
    
*   ⭐️ Exclusively native built for macOS. ElectronJS-based for Windows & Linux
    
*   👑 Comprehensive debugging tools: Compose, Repeat, ...
    
*   🛠 Advanced Tools: Map Local, Map Remote, Breakpoint, Allow List, Block List, External Proxying, No Caching, Clear Cache, Protobuf, Scripting (Rewrite), and Diff.
    
*   👨‍💻 Customizable workspace.
    
*   🖥 Support macOS 12 or later
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/#id-3.-download)

3\. Download


---------------------------------------------------------------

*   Download the latest [macOS app](https://proxyman.io/release/osx/Proxyman_latest.dmg)
    
*   Download the latest [Windows app](https://proxyman.io/release/windows/Proxyman_latest.dmg)
    
*   Download the latest [Linux app](https://proxyman.com/release/linux/proxyman_latest)
    
*   Download the latest [iOS app](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695)
    
*   Download via Cask
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/#id-4.-github)

4\. Github


-----------------------------------------------------------

[Proxyman's Repo Github](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman)
 is where you can create tickets for feature requests, discussions, or report bugs and catch up with Proxyman's team quickly and efficiently.

We welcome all bug reports and feature requests 😍

If you'd notify all Proxyman's release. Please watch the repo

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/#id-4.-milestone)

4\. Milestone


-----------------------------------------------------------------

 in the GitHub repo.

[NextChangelog](https://docs.proxyman.com/changelog)

# Proxyman for iOS | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#id-1.-proxyman-for-ios)

1\. Proxyman for iOS


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#features)

Features

*   ✅ Capture all network traffic (HTTP/HTTPS) from your iOS Devices (No Macbook required).
    
*   Proxyman for iOS is a **standalone** app and works **independently** with Proxyman for macOS.
    
*   View HTTP/HTTPS Requests and Responses in plain text.
    
*   FaceID and Passcode to protect your sensitive data.
    
*   Share logs to Proxyman for macOS.
    
*   Split View (Two Side Panel) for iPad.
    
*   Debugging Tool: Map Local, Breakpoint, Block List, SSL Proxying List, No Caching.
    
*   and more...
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#download)

Download

*   AppStore: [https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695)
    
*   Requires iOS 15+
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#screenshots)

Screenshots

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FBAtNZVxLaZ9RIjOYtQxS%252FScreenshot%25202023-06-01%2520at%252015.28.38.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df08ac6bf-723c-4043-92bd-319643265d32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6367f0e2&sv=2)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F48eBMi75DxDraPiZozJS%252FScreenshot%25202023-06-01%2520at%252015.28.42.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D965254ef-a776-498a-8ff8-e1cd11746250&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3507b38d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#id-2.-proxyman-vpn)

2\. Proxyman VPN


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#how-does-it-work)

How does it work?

Proxyman for iOS creates a local VPN on your devices, then proxying all traffic from your iOS devices to a local Man-In-The-Middle Server.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#what-data-does-proxyman-use)

What data does Proxyman use?

1.  **HTTP/HTTPS Request and Response data**
    

Proxyman captures and decrypts HTTP/HTTPS data (Including Headers, Body, URL, Host, etc )to display them in plain text

2\. **Device Name**

To generate a self-signed Root Certificate. Proxyman does not use pre-generated or shared certificates.

Proxyman records the request/response data and stores it on the l**ocal SQLite database** in your iOS Devices.

Proxyman **does not send** your data to any remote servers or third parties.

Your data always remains **private** to you.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/vpn-and-proxyman-certificate#id-3.-activate-premium-proxyman-for-ios)

3\. Activate Premium Proxyman for iOS


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a valid macOS License, you can unlock Premium Proxyman for iOS. 1 seat can redeem for 2 iOS Devices.

To activate, please Download Proxyman for iOS (AppStore) -> Open More Tab (on the Right-Bottom TabBar) -> FaceID & Passcode -> Unlock -> Enter your license key.

[PreviousSecurity Compliance](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance)
[NextMap Local for iOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/map-local-for-ios)

# License | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#proxyman-pro)

Proxyman Pro


--------------------------------------------------------------------

You can try all debugging tools with the Trial version, which is limited to 2 pinned domains, 2 rules for each debugging tool, and no new tabs.

The **Pro version** comes with:

*   A year’s worth of macOS, Windows, and Linux updates
    
*   1 Mac device per seat
    
*   Premium [Proxyman for iOS](https://proxyman.io/ios)
     (2 devices per seat)
    
*   Multiple Tabs
    
*   Unlimited Pinned Domains / Apps
    
*   Unlimited rules for all Advanced Debugging Tools (e.g., [SSL Proxying List](https://docs.proxyman.io/basic-features/ssl-proxying)
    , [Map Local](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/map-local)
    , [Map Remote](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/map-remote)
    , [Breakpoint](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/breakpoint)
    , [Allow/Block List](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/blacklist)
    , [Protobuf](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/protobuf)
    , [Scripting](https://docs.proxyman.io/scripting/script)
    , [Network Conditions](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/network-throttling)
    , [Multiple Filters](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/multiple-filters)
    , [Reverse Proxy](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/reverse-proxy)
    , [Request/Response Diff](https://docs.proxyman.io/advanced-features/diff)
    , etc).
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#trial-evaluation-duration)

Trial Evaluation Duration


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Personal Purpose: No time limit.
    
*   Business Purpose: It's for 2 weeks. After that, please consider purchasing the license.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#demo-key)

Demo Key


------------------------------------------------------------

If you're a team/company, you can request a 2-week demo key, then please contact [\[email protected\]](https://docs.proxyman.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#buy-proxyman-license)

Buy Proxyman License


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please navigate to the [Pricing page](https://proxyman.io/pricing)
 for purchasing Proxyman Licenses.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#manage-proxyman-license)

Manage Proxyman License


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're the owner of the Proxyman license key, you can manage your devices by using the [License Manager](https://docs.proxyman.com/license-manager)
.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#active-license)

Active License


------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#macos-windows-linux-app)

macOS/Windows/Linux app

1.  After purchasing the Proxyman License, you will receive a license key in your mailbox.
    
2.  To activate, please open the Proxyman app (macOS/Windows/Linux) -> Proxyman Menu -> Buy Proxyman Pro.
    
3.  Click on the "Activate License" button and enter your license key
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FmEVEggLP5ERnkjYaf691%252FScreenshot%25202024-02-18%2520at%252009.20.49.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99272b6f-4dbe-4945-8f52-a0f37a21ece7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f8761be8&sv=2)

Activate License Key on macOS/Windows/Linux app

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#activate-the-license-key-with-your-corporate-proxy)

Activate the License key with your Corporate proxy

*   Available from Proxyman macOS 5.5.0 or later
    
*   Some companies have a Corporate Proxy, so can't activate the license key. To make it work, please follow the guide below:
    

1.  Open Tools -> Proxy Setting -> External Proxy
    
2.  Check "Enable External Proxy Tool"
    
3.  Check the HTTP and HTTPS checkboxes
    
4.  For each HTTP and HTTPS: Enter your Proxy Host and Port.
    
5.  If your corporate proxy has the authentication, please enter it.
    
6.  Done ✅
    
7.  Try to activate the License Key again.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FpBtSt61aJytpsLfFKSqG%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-03%2520at%252015.05.31%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1452ab4a-7990-4000-83c7-0a60b8cd389c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4b7781f3&sv=2)

How to use External Proxy to Activate Proxyman License key

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#ios-app)

iOS app

Proxyman license key comes with the Proxyman iOS app. 1 seat can be activated on 2 iOS devices.

1.  Download the iOS app at App Store: [https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman-network-debug-tool/id1551292695](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman-network-debug-tool/id1551292695)
    
2.  Open the More Tab (on the Right-Bottom TabBar) -> FaceID & Passcode -> Unlock -> Enter your license key.
    
3.  Done
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#activate-license-by-cli-macos-only)

Activate License by CLI (macOS Only)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you have a huge number of licenses, you would like to have an automatic way to activate a license. You can do it too.

1.  Download the Proxyman app and copy it to the `/Applications` folder
    
2.  **Open and close the app at least.** It's necessary to set up some configurations.
    
3.  Open Terminal and execute the following cmd:
    

To **Activate**:

To **Unlink** device:

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-Mgdp1dMRwpP2wX_ZYK0%252F-MgdpIilgkRX37KnFBtu%252F128307433-8887f444-5c94-42bb-8ec6-f30bce271f50.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df36c27bc-1d8b-4c67-9577-580203cc2d84&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a2065b0e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#activate-by-url)

Activate by URL

You can also activate a Proxyman license by the URL:

1.  Download and open Proxyman at least 1 time.
    
2.  Open the URL in Safari or Google Chrome.
    

`proxyman://activate?key=<key>`

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#remove-license)

Remove License

You can remove your license from your devices and then activate it on your new devices as long as you have enough available seats.

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#from-your-current-devices)

From your current devices

Open Proxyman app -> Proxyman Menu -> License -> Click on the "Unlink this device" button.

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#with-license-manager)

With License Manager

1.  Open the [License Manager](https://proxyman.io/license-manager/access-link)
    
2.  Enter the email address that you've used to purchase a license
    
3.  Open the access link from your email.
    
4.  Click on the device to remove it.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license#activate-license-with-cooperated-proxy-server)

Activate License with Cooperated Proxy Server

From Proxyman 4.12.0 or later, you can ask Proxyman to use Cooperated Proxy in a Tools Menu -> Proxy Setting -> External Proxy -> Set HTTP / HTTPS Proxy setting.

# Command-line | Proxyman

Proxyman provides a useful command-line tool to enhance your onboarding experience ✅.

You can access the tool at `/Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli`

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-1.-export-proxyman-config)

1\. Export Proxyman config


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Export all debugging tools rules, such as SSL Proxying List, Breakpoint, Map Local, Scripting, Block List, Allow List, Reverse Proxy, and Network Conditions.

Copy

    $ /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export -h
    
    OVERVIEW: Export all debugging tools rules (Breakpoint, SSL Pinning, Map Local, Map
    Remote, Scripting, etc).
    
    USAGE: proxyman-cli export [--mode <mode>] --output <output>
    
    OPTIONS:
      -m, --mode <mode>       Export Mode (all = "All debugging tools's rules", enabledRules
                              = "Only enabled rules"). (default: all)
      -o, --output <output>   A Output file to save the config to.
      --version               Show the version.
      -h, --help              Show help information.

By default, the `export` command will export all rules. To exclude particular rules, please uncheck the "Enabled" column in each debugging tool and use the `-m enabledRules`

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#for-example)

For example:

*   Export all debugging tool rules:
    

`$ /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export -o ~/Desktop/data.json`

*   Only export enabled rules:
    

`$ /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export -m enabledRules -o ~/Desktop/data.json`

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-2.-import-proxyman-config)

2\. Import Proxyman config


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Import Proxyman debugging tools rules that you have exported by the export command.

By default, new imported rules will be appended to the existing debugging rules. To override all rules, let use `-m override`

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#for-example-1)

For example:

*   Import all debugging rules by appending them:
    

*   Import, but override all my existing rules:
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-3.-activate-unlink-license)

3\. Activate/Unlink License


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please check out the command for activating and unlinking a license.

[License](https://docs.proxyman.com/license)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-4.-toggle-http-system-proxy)

4\. Toggle HTTP System Proxy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 4.8.0 and later, we can toggle the Proxy System by command line. It's useful for Raycast Extension

Reference: [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1626#issuecomment-1545862020](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1626#issuecomment-1545862020)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-5.-clear-session)

5\. Clear Session


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   We can clear the current Session from the command line. Available for Proxyman 4.12.0 and later.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-6.-toggle-debugging-tools)

6\. Toggle Debugging Tools


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Toggle Breakpoint, Map Local, and Scripting Tool by command line. Available for Proxyman 4.12.0 and later.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-7.-install-the-proxy-helper-tool-by-command-line)

7\. Install the Proxy Helper Tool by command line


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From macOS 4.12.0 or later, you can install the Helper Tool without GUI.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-8.-export-proxyman-log)

8\. Export Proxyman Log


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**Proxyman macOS v5.11.0+ now supports:**

*   Export all (ProxymanSession Format)
    

*   Export certain domains (Only Host, no scheme, no port, no paths, and no Query)
    

**From Proxyman macOS 5.20.0+, we can export with Raw or HAR format.**

*   Export All - RAW Request/Response Format
    

*   Export All - HAR Format
    

*   Export certain domains - RAW Request/Response Format
    

*   Export certain domains - HAR Format
    

**From macOS 6.2.0+, we can export with a flag** `**--since <last_flow_id>**` **to only export from this flow ID.**

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#id-9.-import-custom-root-certificate)

9\. Import Custom Root Certificate


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ✅ Import Custom p12 Root Certificate to Proxyman
    
*   Automatically Trust the certificate in System Keychain (sudo required)
    
*   Available from Proxyman macOS 5.15.0 or later
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#install-and-trust)

Install and trust

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/command-line#install-but-not-trust-you-might-need-to-trust-it-manually-in-the-keychain)

Install but not trust (you might need to trust it manually in the Keychain)

[NextSecurity Compliance](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance)

Copy

    $ /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli import -h
    
    OVERVIEW: Import config to Proxyman.
    
    USAGE: proxyman-cli import [--mode <mode>] --input <input>
    
    OPTIONS:
      -m, --mode <mode>       Import Mode (append = "Append to the existing rules"),
                              override = "Import and Replace all existing rules". (default:
                              append)
      -i, --input <input>     A input file to import.
      --version               Show the version.
      -h, --help              Show help information.

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli import -i ~/Desktop/data.json

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli import -m override -i ~/Desktop/data.json

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli proxy on
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli proxy off

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli clear-session

Copy

    # Scripting
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli scripting on
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli scripting off
    
    # Map Local
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli maplocal on
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli maplocal off
    
    # Breakpoint
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli breakpoint on
    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli breakpoint off

Copy

    sudo /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman --install-privileged-components

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m all -o "~/desktop/output"

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m domains -o "~/desktop/output" --domains 'api.twitter.com' --domains 'www.producthunt.com'

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m all -o "~/desktop/output" --format raw

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m domains -o "~/desktop/output" --domains 'api.twitter.com' --domains 'www.producthunt.com' --format har

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m all -o "~/desktop/output" --format raw

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli export-log -m domains -o "~/desktop/output" --domains 'api.twitter.com' --domains 'www.producthunt.com' --format raw

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli install-root-cert <certificate_path> --password <your_cert_password> --trust

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/MacOS/proxyman-cli install-root-cert <certificate_path> --password <your_cert_password>

# License Manager | Proxyman

License Manager is an easier way to manage your license, which allows you to:

*   Display License status (Purchase date, Expiry date, Number of Mac / iOS Seats)
    
*   See a list of devices, which activated by your license key
    
*   Renew / Extend your license key
    
*   Remove Mac or iOS devices
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FvdaVyomfECUnSQAdADNH%252FProxyman_License_Manager.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D673f5de0-27ff-4beb-b7dd-96900948c9d5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e42c5793&sv=2)

License Manager

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/license-manager#how-to-use-it)

How to use it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open the [License Manage](https://proxyman.io/license-manager/access-link)
    
2.  Enter your email, which you purchase a license key.
    
3.  You will receive a `Access Link` from your mailbox.
    
4.  Open it to access the License Manager.
    

If you don't remember which email you purchase Proxyman License, please contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.proxyman.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

[PreviousLicense](https://docs.proxyman.com/license)
[NextRaycast](https://docs.proxyman.com/raycast)

# Breakpoint for iOS | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/breakpoint-for-ios#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Breakpoint is a tool to help developers:

*   Modify the Request Content: URL, Method, Header, and the Body
    
*   Modify the Response Content: Status Code, Headers, and the Body
    

on the fly, without depending on Proxyman for macOS.

# Map Local for iOS | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/map-local-for-ios#whats-it)

What's it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Map Local is a tool to help iOS developers to:

*   Map the URL with any pre-defined Response. It allows you to quickly test out with new Response without waiting for the real Endpoint from your Backend Server.
    
*   You can modify the Status Code, Headers, and Body.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FL8DWGalWnBlQYrD15OBF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22d84080-d47c-460f-8bbc-69f91af794c5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7adbba9a&sv=2)

# Security Compliance | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#exciting-news-proxyman-achieves-soc-2-type-2-compliance)

Exciting News: Proxyman Achieves SOC 2 Type 2 Compliance!

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FHPEnIvKEiaU20KquIGkU%252FFrame%25208.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dacd187c8-36c9-46e7-9653-470db4a0eb49&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc630e6e&sv=2)

Proxyman is now SOC 2 Compliant

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#what-is-soc-2-type-2-compliance)

What is SOC 2 Type 2 Compliance?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

SOC 2 is a stringent audit by the AICPA. A Type 1 report confirms our security controls are well-designed at a specific time, evaluating five key criteria:

*   **Security**: Protects against unauthorized access.
    
*   **Availability**: Ensures system availability for use.
    
*   **Processing Integrity**: Guarantees complete and accurate processing.
    
*   **Confidentiality**: Safeguards confidential information.
    
*   **Privacy**: Handles personal data per our privacy policy.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#why-soc-2-type-2-compliance-matters)

Why SOC 2 Type 2 Compliance Matters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In today's digital world, strong security is essential. For a debugging proxy tool managing sensitive data, SOC 2 compliance:

*   Validates security controls.
    
*   Shows commitment to data protection.
    
*   Offers independent verification.
    
*   Demonstrates adherence to industry standards.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#what-does-this-mean-for-you)

What Does This Mean for You?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#as-a-customer)

**As a Customer**

*   **Enhanced Security**: Your data enjoys robust protection.
    
*   **Privacy Assurance**: Your information is handled responsibly.
    
*   **Transparency**: Security practices are verified.
    
*   **Trust**: Confidently use Proxyman in enterprises.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#as-a-reseller)

**As a Reseller**

*   **Credibility**: Assure customers of our security.
    
*   **Enterprise-Ready**: Easily recommended to security-focused organizations.
    
*   **Compliance**: Meet vendor assessment needs.
    
*   **Documentation**: Access for sales support.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#privacy-statement)

Privacy Statement


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#you-can-find-our-privacy-policy)

You can find our [Privacy Policy](https://proxyman.io/privacy)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/security-compliance#whats-next)

What's Next?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This milestone is the first step. Our focus includes:

*   Maintain SOC 2 Type 2 compliance.
    
*   Conducting regular audits.
    
*   Continuously enhancing security practices.
    

For more about our security and privacy policies, visit our Privacy Policy, Terms of Service, and SDLC Policy. Questions? Reach us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.proxyman.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

# Map Local for iOS Tutorial | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#manipulate-http-s-response-on-iphone-using-proxyman-map-local-tool)

M**anipulate HTTP(s) response on iPhone using Proxyman Map Local Tool**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Since version 2.0.0, Proxyman has introduced Map Local Tool which enables developers to use the content of local files as a response to your requests, as they match with your rules.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F6ZkLy5DOt15zfy8h9Rzf%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd07770db-26f5-4cb4-bfdc-a75947157a81&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39dfa7aa&sv=2)

Map Local Tool could significantly boost your speed development and provide the capability to rapidly test on several edge-cased without explicitly updating the data in your server. It’s also the must-have tool for QAs or Developers if you would like to test the app’s behavior with various responses. Some of the testing scenarios:

*   Define a Response and use it as a Response for matched Requests
    
*   Quickly try new parameters in responses.
    
*   Test the app’s behaviors with different parameters in the responses.
    
*   Test the UI layout with unusual content.
    
*   Quickly reproduce the bug with specific parameters in responses.
    
*   Mock Fake API with a local File: It's useful for developers would try out the testing APIs which are not in production.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Already downloaded the latest version of Proxyman on AppStore: [https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695)
    
*   Already installed and trusted Proxyman Certificate on iOS device (If you’re new to Proxyman, please follow [this tutorial](https://proxyman.io/posts/2021-10-17-Getting-Started-With-Proxyman-For-iOS)
     on how to start intercepting HTTP traffic on your iPhone).
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#create-map-local-rules)

Create Map Local Rules


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 2 ways that we can define a Breakpoint rule:

1.  From Setting screen
    

*   Go to Setting → map Local → Tap on + button.
    
*   From here we will need to manually fill in all required fields for the Rule, including Title, Method, Matching URL, and include Subpaths or not.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FqBB6jjw5emTe4sQ5BYXT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D34ae2ba7-78a7-4aa5-962e-8f3f29f24aa5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a61953d6&sv=2)

1.  From the Menu context
    

*   Long tap on the Request → Add to Map Local List.
    
*   It will automatically fill in all fields to define the Rule based on the selected Request.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FP4m6fwmDFFajCiM7XFor%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D778aced2-f42f-4733-af3f-bbff9d6e0b40&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6ec04f1&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#modify-header-status-code-and-body)

Modify Header, Status Code and Body

From the Map Local Editor screen, we can freely manipulate the Headers, Status Code and Body data. If we alternate the Body with the new data type, Proxyman will auto-detect the Content-Type and update Headers for us.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FKpKjXE8Lb8rKElzA1VbI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dda5cfafe-853b-47f0-bdfb-220ca74a7946&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=12aea40&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#manipulate-response-with-map-local-tool)

Manipulate Response with Map Local Tool


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FUOsK4RcZW2hkNf12zj39%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D59fc799c-5ea7-4ac8-b811-fc0c8be49096&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9820ddb4&sv=2)

And you’re all set, it’s time to make another request to see how it works.

If the URL of incoming requests are matching with the **pre-defined matching Rule**, and the Local file is valid => The body response of those matching requests is automatically replaced with the content of the local file.

If the requests are not matching any rules, the entire Response's content remains on the server.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEc0h4lMACaiTWXE5nfc4%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf9e5161-be5a-4438-a184-6018415bab7e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=329c0ac4&sv=2)

Nicely done! If you look into the flow list, you will find a small blue icon to indicate that this flow has been modified. As you can see, both the Response content has been updated with the local file.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#whats-next)

What’s next


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Map Local tool allows you to try various types of responses to test the layout or content from your devices, thus boosting your debugging productivity, but limited by the capability of modifying Response content only. If you'd like to modify the Request content, you might want to check out our [Breakpoint tutorial](https://docs.proxyman.io/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial)
 that enables us to manipulate both the Request and Response on the fly without changing any logic from your client.

[PreviousTutorial for iOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios)
[NextBreakpoint for iOS Tutorial](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [Manipulate HTTP(s) response on iPhone using Proxyman Map Local Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#manipulate-http-s-response-on-iphone-using-proxyman-map-local-tool)
    
*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#prerequisites)
    
*   [Create Map Local Rules](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#create-map-local-rules)
    
*   [Manipulate Response with Map Local Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#manipulate-response-with-map-local-tool)
    
*   [What’s next](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial#whats-next)

# Breakpoint for iOS Tutorial | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#modify-http-s-request-and-response-on-your-iphone-with-proxyman-breakpoint-tool)

M**odify HTTP(s) Request & Response on your iPhone with Proxyman Breakpoint Tool**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Since version 2.0.0, Proxyman has introduced a new feature that enables developers to manipulate the Request & Response data on the fly without changing any logic from your client.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FBIZoWcR4stO85CRcpmxs%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c91591e-bb3b-4c14-88cc-2dbd9ec5861b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a770a8b6&sv=2)

This mini tutorial demonstrates how we can modify HTTP(s) Requests/Responses on iOS devices with Proxyman Breakpoint Tool, for example:

*   Modify the Request URL (including the Scheme, Host, Path, Port) and HTTP Method
    
*   Modify HTTP Headers of Request/Response
    
*   Modify Query from Requests
    
*   Modify HTTP Body of Request/Response
    
*   Modify Response HTTP Status Code
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#prerequisites)

Prerequisites


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Already downloaded the latest version of Proxyman on AppStore: [https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695](https://apps.apple.com/us/app/proxyman/id1551292695)
    
*   Already installed and trusted Proxyman Certificate on iOS device (If you’re new to Proxyman, please follow [this tutorial](https://proxyman.io/posts/2021-10-17-Getting-Started-With-Proxyman-For-iOS)
     on how to start intercepting HTTP traffic on your iPhone).
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#create-breakpoint-rules)

Create Breakpoint Rules


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are 3 ways that we can define a Breakpoint rule:

1.  From Setting screen
    

*   Go to Setting → Breakpoint → Tap on the + button.
    
*   From here we will need to manually fill in all required fields for the Rule, including Title, Method, Matching URL, and include Subpaths or not.
    
*   We are also able to select if this rule is applied for upcoming Requests, Responses or both.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F5S4NyNWNB3xFvEJc08zr%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd4210feb-66b7-45ce-84c4-f05003d088f5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=793d65b1&sv=2)

1.  From "Waiting Breakpoint" screen
    

*   Tap on Waiting Breakpoint icon → Create Breakpoint Rule.
    
*   Then we will need to manually create the Rule (similar to the previous option).
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FxlSs0vWcERciw078gyrF%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee2968a9-c897-4304-9b21-6a7fb4473266&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=aca6b8ce&sv=2)

1.  From the Menu context
    

*   Long tap on the Request → Add to Breakpoint List.
    
*   It will automatically fill in all fields to define the Rule based on the selected Request.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FQNBr7U0CDx115BSJ2zs6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc435835e-625d-4002-8dfa-d6006b032af8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=83e6f8bb&sv=2)

In this example, the Breakpoint Rule will apply to both upcoming Requests/ Responses. Let’s make a Request to see how it works.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEpsjclwDCDZQ7hjGg6Q0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33dbcbe4-98a7-487c-bd8e-957f662ede49&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7c7303e4&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#modify-http-s-requests)

Modify HTTP(s) Requests


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once we make a Request with the matching URL, Proxyman will stop it and notify us that there are waiting breakpoints. From the Home screen, we can tap the small icon to see the waiting Breakpoint list and select a Breakpoint to start modifying the Request Content.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FJJC63T0lDdXd092MbXPw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b68af10-38b6-4e84-93f6-b7d2656d0bba&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0aef556&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#modify-url--method)

Modify URL + Method

We can freely manipulate the HTTP Method, URL, and Query,. The URL will be auto-updated as the queries change and vice versa.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F9mVthwRmJf5DWqU1l756%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd9ba8a2f-9156-4ede-a6b0-e40916a9893a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1964cd3c&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#modify-body)

Modify Body

If we alternate the Body with a new data type, Proxyman will auto-detect the Content-Type and update Headers for us.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F7GfNV7zNrQfhmjn7DwRo%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80159dd2-ac02-4759-aa84-7b1ff5511858&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f15d386b&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#execute-abort-continue-breakpoint)

Execute, abort, continue Breakpoint


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

When you're happy with the change, you can execute the Request/ Response by selecting the option from the top right menu. To keep the original Request, you can use the Continue button or cancel it with the Abort option.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEvLV3vQCd1maOUfvAXXZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D64c6a7c9-0237-4b82-8357-4043ff119d29&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4d2eb1&sv=2)

Since our Breakpoint rule is applied for both Request and Response, you will find the Response added to waiting breakpoints list once you hit the “Execute” button.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FfyYSzntonxkmLbpD7TFj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D92c65c2a-8be6-4d60-9d52-fcbedfb5fa16&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8f135ca4&sv=2)

Now you can change the HTTP Status Code, update Headers or alternate the Body with new content for Response (similar to modifying Request Breakpoint)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F6HJlMZouZ9Rf4Biq7XOK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61f4963f-e9a2-415b-bfc4-090e9574acd4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43974d97&sv=2)

Nicely done! If you look into the flow list, you will find a small blue icon to indicate that this flow has been modified.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FAuspFYIailtEHGC27hVe%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da35c9593-caa4-44b5-8d11-b9da9beec27c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7963374a&sv=2)

As you can see, both the Request and Response content has been updated as expected.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fcl0SHf0RIWtAuJnScERy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcf18c528-9673-4802-8459-d667eece41ff&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4292ccf5&sv=2)

**NOTES**:

*   When you create a new rule, both Breakpoint Tool and Rule will be enabled by default (you can switch it ON/OFF as needed).
    
*   Make sure to check the VPN status (1), the Breakpoint Tool status (2), and the Breakpoint Rule status (3) are all ENABLED so that the Breakpoint Tool can work.
    
*   If the first rule matches the Requests/ Responses, other rules will not be applied.
    
*   As you’re editing the Request, the Response tab will be disabled. As you’re editing the Response, the Request tab will be displayed in read-only mode.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#whats-next)

What’s next


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Breakpoint allows you to modify the Request/Response on the fly, but it requires a lot of manual works. If you'd like to make it automated, you might check out our [Map Local tool](https://docs.proxyman.io/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial)
 tutorial to automatically map a local file as a Response.

[PreviousMap Local for iOS Tutorial](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/map-local-for-ios-tutorial)
[NextmacOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)

*   [Prerequisites](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#prerequisites)
    
*   [Create Breakpoint Rules](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#create-breakpoint-rules)
    
*   [Modify HTTP(s) Requests](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#modify-http-s-requests)
    
*   [Execute, abort, continue Breakpoint](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-ios/tutorial-for-ios/breakpoint-for-ios-tutorial#execute-abort-continue-breakpoint)

# iOS Simulator | Proxyman

In order to capture the HTTP/HTTPS message from your iOS Simulator devices, please navigate to:

*   **Certificate** **Menu** -> **Install Certificate on iOS -> Simulators**
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#id-1.-ios-simulator-setup-guide)

1\. iOS Simulator Setup Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FOTHyl34jcJKoxLlftmAv%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202022-07-11%2520at%252008.15.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6c20e89e-e37c-4bc0-a115-bf12ca60c25b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c75fd201&sv=2)

Automatically install the Certificate to iOS Simulators

It works for iOS, iPadOS, tvOS and watchOS.

The following photo describes three steps:

1.  Install **Root Proxyman Certificate** on your machine: You can follow the [macOS Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)
    .
    
2.  Install Proxyman Certificate to all available simulators, which you have opened at least one time.
    
3.  **Reset the Simulator**: Proxyman tries to reset all simulators, so it will load the new Certificate.
    

From Proxyman 2.19.0+, Proxyman uses the [simctl](https://nshipster.com/simctl/)
 command line to perform tasks.

**simctl** is built-in on your installed Xcode, which is more modern and reliable than the legacy approach (Use Python custom scripts).

This step only installs on Simulators, which you have open at least one time

For instance, if you would like to debug on iPhone X Simulator, please make sure to **open** the iPhone X Simulator first, then **install** the Certificate in Step 2

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#xcode-preview-swiftui)

Xcode Preview (SwiftUI)

If you're using Xcode Preview for SwiftUI, you can install the certificate into the Xcode Preview Simulator by following:

1.  Open Xcode with Previewer Mode (SwiftUI).
    
2.  Open Proxyman -> Certificate Menu -> Install for iOS -> Simulator
    
3.  Click on the Advanced button -> Install for Xcode Preview
    

You can read more at: [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1568#issue-1610877870](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1568#issue-1610877870)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#manually-install)

Manually Install

In Proxyman v4.16.0 or later, you can manually install the certificate to your iOS Simulator in case the Automatic Solution doesn't work.

1.  Certificate Menu -> Install Certificates for iOS -> Simulators
    
2.  In Step 2, click on the ↓ button (Next to the Prepare Simulators button) -> Install Manually…
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FwyIzDnapd10ppD45YJEj%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-01%2520at%252020.14.39.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2de174a8-18aa-4c4a-9af6-042b997ac05f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e5242bde&sv=2)

Install certificate manually

1.  Drag and drop the certificate to your iOS Simulator
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FLG9nNR54513dcoCfEK4k%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-07%2520at%252014.43.13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D28aee8d4-f520-42c2-9943-12c9609758eb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9fefc94&sv=2)

Manually Install the certificate

1.  Open your iOS Simulator -> Setting app -> General -> About -> Certificate Trust Setting -> Find Proxyman CA Certificate and switch it ON
    
2.  Done
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#id-2.-troubleshooting)

2\. Troubleshooting


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#id-1.-unable-to-install-the-certificate)

1\. Unable to install the Certificate

If you get errors when clicking on Step 2, please open Xcode -> Preferences -> Location tabs -> Select your Xcode in the Command Line Tools.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fur9sOsIVGGJmQiPFslqK%252FScreen_Shot_2022-07-11_at_08_12_33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc42927bd-bc3f-4518-b03f-6751ae4943ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=17b159cf&sv=2)

Make sure you have the Xcode Command Line

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#id-2.-get-ssl-error-from-https-response)

2\. Get SSL Error from HTTPS Response

*   Opening the Setting app -> General -> About -> Certificate Trust Settings and verifying that Proxyman Certificate is installed and trusted.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MV039NT2Fefr24GMsvz%252F-MV04a_0MtTevA03M6fq%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-03-05%2520at%252013.32.25.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35fc01cc-2a36-425f-aa80-e83b8ce9fea2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9d8568&sv=2)

Proxyman Certificate is installed and trusted properly

If it's not installed:

*   Open the iOS Simulator Setup (Certificate Menu -> Install Certificate on iOS -> Simulator) and click on the 2nd button.
    
*   Or Try the following step to manually install the Certificate.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#id-3.-some-http-https-requests-are-missing-from-proxyman)

3\. Some HTTP/HTTPS Requests are missing from Proxyman

Alamofire or URLSession might use the cached response for your request. As a result, the actual request doesn't hit the server. Thus, Proxyman could not capture and display it on the app.

Solution:

*   Disable the cache mechanism on URLSession or Alamofre.
    
*   Use the [No Caching Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching)
     (⌥⌘N)
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#manually-install-the-certificate-by-exporting-the-certificate)

Manually Install the Certificate by exporting the certificate


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you cannot install the certificate, you can **manually** do it:

1.  Open Proxyman -> Certificate Menu -> Export -> Root Certificate as DER -> Save to Desktop Folder
    
2.  Open the Simulator **drag the certificate and drop it** on the Simulator screen
    
3.  Open Setting app (on the Simulator) -> General -> Device Management -> Select the Certificate -> Install
    
4.  Setting app -> General -> About -> Certificate Trust Settings and verifying that Proxyman Certificate is installed and trusted.
    
5.  Done ✅
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#tutorial)

Tutorial

See detailed steps to [debug an application on iOS Simulator](https://proxyman.io/blog/2019/07/Debugging-on-iOS-Simulator-with-Proxyman.html)
 with Proxyman

# Java VMs | Proxyman

In order to intercept HTTPS traffic from Java apps, extra steps are required to install the Proxyman CA Certificate into the Java Key Store.

*   Intercept Traffic from Unit Test (written by Java or Kotlin)
    
*   Intercept Traffic from Java app or CLI
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java#id-1.-benefit)

1\. Benefit


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Proxyman provides a script to help developers automatically install Root Certificate to Java KeyStore with 1 click ✅
    
*   Support `$JAVA_HOME`
    
*   Support `SDKMAN`
    
*   Support `/usr/libexec/java_home`
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java#id-2.-how-to-use)

2\. How to use?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java#id-1.-install-proxyman-ca-on-your-mac)

1\. Install Proxyman CA on your Mac

Before installing Proxyman CA on Java VMs, we have to install it properly on your current Mac machine.

Check out the macOS Guideline:

[macOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)

You can skip and start the next step if you've done this step.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java#id-2.-install-proxyman-ca-to-all-java-key-stores)

2\. Install Proxyman CA to all Java Key Stores


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Certificate Menu -> Install Certificate on Java VMs -> Run Scripts
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FGRgqua059Qa4O3GwRCBl%252FScreen_Shot_2022-04-08_at_15_12_49.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a8584e2-9e78-4cb2-8a15-ebec4f988a92&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d2dbe75a&sv=2)

Run Java script

*   The script will attempt to find the Key Store location from **JAVA\_HOME, SDKHOME,** or from **$(/usr/libexec/java\_home)** environment and install the CA Certificate if possible
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FFGnSsCF3yPNokQln4Fgz%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-15%2520at%252014.20.51.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da34d3dac-b820-4e59-9789-5282fcd3e131&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=71b12c27&sv=2)

Proxyman install the certificate to all Java Trust Store if possible

You can find the script at /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Versions/A/Resources/install-certificates-java.sh

The script might require permission for EventKit because Proxyman triggers the script by [Apple Script](https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/documentation/AppleScript/Conceptual/AppleScriptLangGuide/introduction/ASLR_intro.html)
 in order to install it under admin permission.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java#alternative-solution)

Alternative solution

*   Check out @[**yauheniprakapenka**](https://github.com/yauheniprakapenka)
     solution: [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/569#issuecomment-723588490](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/569#issuecomment-723588490)
     if you get the following error
    

`sun.security.validator.ValidatorException: PKIX path building failed: sun.security.provider.certpath.SunCertPathBuilderException: unable to find valid certification path to requested target javax.net.ssl.SSLHandshakeException: sun.security.validator.ValidatorException: PKIX path building failed: sun.security.provider.certpath.SunCertPathBuilderException: unable to find valid certification path to requested target`

[PreviousFirefox](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox)
[NextPython](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/python)

# Firefox | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox#new-solution-proxyman-v5.19.0-or-later-recommended)

✅ New Solution (Proxyman v5.19.0 or later - recommended)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With Proxyman v5.19.0+, Proxyman can capture HTTPS Requests/Responses from Firefox with 1-click setup.

1.  Go to Setup Menu -> Automatic Setup
    
2.  On the Web Browser Section -> Click the ⬇️ Arrow Button -> Select Firefox
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fs9CEz0ITuJFFEjMWYjLG%252FScreenshot%25202025-04-28%2520at%252009.53.27.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D87bc7291-2ecf-418f-9bc5-f58bcbf0c02f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6cc15097&sv=2)

How to capture HTTPS Reqyests/Responses from Firefox Browser with Proxyman

1.  New Firefox instance will open
    
2.  ✅ Done. All traffic from Firefox will be captured by Proxyman
    

This setup will make Firefox or Google Chrome:

*   Auto set Proxyman to Proxyman
    
*   Auto install & trust Proxyman Certificate
    

Works with Google Chrome and Firefox

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox#old-solution-proxyman-v5.18.0-or-ealier)

❌ Old Solution (Proxyman v5.18.0 or ealier)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In order to intercept HTTPS traffic from Firefox, it requires extra steps to install Proxyman CA into Firefox's Trust Store.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox#id-1.-install-proxyman-ca-on-macos-machine)

1\. Install Proxyman CA on macOS machine

Before installing Proxyman CA on Java VMs, we have to install it properly on your current machine.

Check out macOS Guidelines:

[macOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)

If you've done this step, you can skip to the next step.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox#id-2.-set-proxy-on-firefox)

2\. Set Proxy on Firefox

*   Open Firefox's Preferences panel (CMD+,)
    
*   Search Proxy and open the Proxy Settings
    
*   Select Auto Use System Proxy or manually hardcode the Proxy IP and Port
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MH_Go0N5xZXL5IXWXr0%252F-MH_Hi8ciXNj2TC6323L%252FScreen_Shot_2020-09-19_at_14_33_17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D893e85c2-2e4a-451b-b4b0-eccfa1446280&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9127de2f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox#id-3.-install-proxyman-ca-to-firefox)

3\. Install Proxyman CA to Firefox

1.  Open `http://proxy.man/ssl` on Firefox and download the certificate to your Download folder
    

http://proxy.man/ssl is a local HTTP Server for strengthening the security. Please make sure the Proxyman app is open when accessing this domain.

2\. Open Firefox's Preferences (CMD+,) and openthe View Certificate window

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MAUFPily_DmIzAplEmx%252F-MAUH9ID3Ks0R5MuU0L6%252FScreen_Shot_2020-06-23_at_10_27_27.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc82c8345-0dae-4fed-bcac-2b9da5ec2f50&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=144251a8&sv=2)

3\. Open the Authorities Tab and select the Import button

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MAUFPily_DmIzAplEmx%252F-MAUHITJp-gj9-hSheNW%252FScreen_Shot_2020-06-23_at_10_27_35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Defc6c514-3041-4499-a3a5-8a071b1fc261&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a64afed&sv=2)

4\. Select Proxyman CA, which you've downloaded and Trust all.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MAUFPily_DmIzAplEmx%252F-MAUHTWo97fQnsijXTbu%252FScreen_Shot_2020-06-23_at_10_37_52.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da88b32e7-e8bf-40b9-a571-7aee82663b28&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31003df3&sv=2)

5\. Reload the page that you need to intercept. Enjoy!

# tvOS & watchOS | Proxyman

Proxyman can capture and intercept HTTP/HTTPS traffic from tvOS and watchOS.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#id-1.-watchos)

1\. watchOS


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#simulator)

Simulator

It's straightforward by following the [Proxyman iOS Simulator Guideline.](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator#ios-simulator-setup-guide)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#watchos-physical-device)

watchOS Physical Device

Follow the [iOS devices guideline](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-device)
 to set HTTP Proxy and install the certificate to your host device.

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#tutorial)

Tutorial:

[![Logo](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fproxyman.com%2Ffavicon%2Fapple-touch-icon.png%3Fv%3D4&width=20&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8607a8ca&sv=2)Intercept HTTPS Network Traffic from WatchOS 26 Simulator (Update for 2025) · ProxymanProxyman](https://proxyman.io/posts/2021-09-02-intercept-https-traffic-from-watch-os-simulator)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#id-2.-tvos)

2\. tvOS


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#simulator-1)

Simulator

Fortunately, it's easy to capture traffic from the tvOS simulator. All you have to do is follow the [iOS Simulator Guideline](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator)
.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/tvos-and-watchos#tvos-devices)

tvOS Devices

It's quite tricky to use Proxyman on a real device.

✅ New Setup Guide (2024)

*   Follow this Medium article (from Raxit Majithiya): **Setup Proxyman in a physical AppleTV** [https://medium.com/@rax/setup-proxyman-in-a-physical-appletv-bf6df86d3a28](https://medium.com/@rax/setup-proxyman-in-a-physical-appletv-bf6df86d3a28)
    

⚠️ Old Setup Guide

1.  Follow this tutorial: [https://www.willowtreeapps.com/craft/a-how-to-guide-for-apple-tv-setup-with-charles-proxy](https://www.willowtreeapps.com/craft/a-how-to-guide-for-apple-tv-setup-with-charles-proxy)
    
2.  Instead of using Charles Proxy, you can use Proxyman.
    

*   Please note that Proxyman port is 9090 (default)
    
*   Export Proxyman Certificate in the Certificate Menu -> Export
    
*   Make sure you install & trust the Proxyman Certificate before intercepting HTTPS Traffic.
    

If you can't set up Proxyman with watchOS or tvOS, please contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.proxyman.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)

# Automatic Script for Android Emulator | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's too complicated and error-prone if we manually override the HTTP Proxy, Install, and Trust Proxyman Certificate from your Android Emulator.

Thus, Proxyman provides a built-in script to automatically perform it in a second. You can access it from **Certificate Menu -> Install Certificate on Android -> Emulator.**

From Proxyman 5.14.0 or earlier, this Script only installs the User Certificate to the User Certificate Store, not the System Certificate Store. If you'd like to install the certificate into the System Certificate, please follow this [tutorial](https://docs.mitmproxy.org/stable/howto-install-system-trusted-ca-android/)
.

From Proxyman 5.15.0 or later, Proxyman can now install Proxyman certificate into the system-level Store. Make it possible to decrypt all HTTPS from Android Emulators.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-2.-benefit)

2\. Benefit?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**1 Click to:**

*   **✅ Auto** Override / Revert HTTP Proxy
    
*   **✅ Automatically** download, install, and trust the Proxyman Certificate at the system-level store. Can decrypt all HTTPS from your Emulators. (Available on Proxyman 5.16.0 or later)
    
*   No need **network\_security\_config.xml**
    
*   **✅** Less error-prone and finishes in a few clicks
    

Work with Android Emulator and Android Physical Devices via \`adb\` (Only for Proxyman v5.19.0+)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FYUJTdlDcvMbE7oM9TZek%252FCapture_HTTPS_Android_Emulator_proxyman.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f8587d7-9d7c-4846-bb71-4469ecdf3c47&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f118e650&sv=2)

Capture and decrypt HTTPS from Android Emulators with Proxyman

*   Install Proxyman Certificate to the system-level Store.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fc1qcfN9TMK2DnivWh8gl%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-10%2520at%252015.12.07.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd05bde13-305d-449a-8579-22056b93e40d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=971f681c&sv=2)

Install Proxyman Certificate to the system-level Store.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-3.-how-to-use-it)

3\. How to use it?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Make sure the adb command is installed. If not, please install it
    

1.  Open your Android app with Android Studio
    
2.  Create a new Emulator in Android Virtual Device Manager. **Make sure it's not the Play Store. Must be a Google Play API**
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MJzb_a8r96FpiHq_Yo9%252F-MJzcil8BjBKKzfatnn9%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-19_at_13_50_31.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df9d6c925-e500-4ec7-93e5-b32e8b248936&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8d073f6b&sv=2)

Create new Google APIs Android Emulators

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MJzb_a8r96FpiHq_Yo9%252F-MJzcnRTL09sMj7o_p8d%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-19_at_13_50_48.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dffdc73bb-7f5d-4404-99b1-e6e0e8f41b1f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5d2a6f90&sv=2)

Create a new Emulator (Google APIs)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FQdOCpbOsA2DREmFdJUKs%252FScreenshot%25202025-09-19%2520at%252020.01.37.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0758e3db-8c09-4f9f-b4fa-d433b1a731e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f2dc7719&sv=2)

1.  Open Proxyman -> Certificate Menu -> Install Certificate on Android -> Emulators -> Click on the Override All Emulators button
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FM3UP3bdIeoflOJDeq8WA%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-10%2520at%252014.54.51.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3084ac09-8fe4-4c83-8f5e-01dfc720ece9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=43455aad&sv=2)

capture all HTTPS from Emulators with 1 click

1.  Wait until the Terminal completes
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FJm2lRgrHDLoZA1mb5NKA%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-10%2520at%252015.02.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbc131b8c-97a9-4294-99f4-7131eed81904&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5803ea66&sv=2)

1.  Relaunch your Android app on Android Studio
    
2.  Proxyman will capture all HTTPS data ✅
    

If you close Proxyman, make sure to click on the Revert All Changes button. Otherwise, your Android Emulator could not access the Internet.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-4.-proxyman-5.15.0-or-earlier)

4\. ⚠️ Proxyman 5.15.0 or earlier


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Proxyman 5.15.0 or earlier is only able to install Proxyman Certificate to the User level.
    
*   It means: We have to complete the next step:
    
*   In your source code:
    
    *   Add res/xml/network\_security\_config.xml
        
    

*   Add to AndroidManifest.xml
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-5.-advance-run-the-script-manually)

5\. Advance: Run the script manually


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's possible to execute the script manually in your Terminal app without granting the Automation Permission in Security & Privacy.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#script-path)

**Script path**:

*   For Proxyman 51.9.0 or later
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#prepare-the-certificate)

Prepare the certificate

1.  Open the Proxyman app
    
2.  Find the current IP in the Main Toolbar
    
3.  Certificate menu -> Export -> Root Certificate as PEM -> Save to Desktop folder
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-4.1-override-http-proxy-and-install-the-certificate-to-system-level-store)

4.1 Override HTTP Proxy and Install the Certificate to system-level Store

*   Proxyman v5.19.0 or later (NEW)
    

*   Proxyman v5.18.0 or earlier
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-4.2-only-override-http-proxy)

4.2 Only Override HTTP Proxy

*   Proxyman v5.19.0 or later (NEW)
    

*   Proxyman v5.18.0 or earlier
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#id-4.3-revert-http-proxy)

4.3 Revert HTTP Proxy

*   Proxyman v5.19.0 or later (NEW)
    

*   Proxyman v5.18.0 or earlier

Copy

    brew install android-platform-tools

Copy

    <network-security-config>
        <debug-overrides>
            <trust-anchors>
                <!-- Trust user added CAs while debuggable only -->
                <certificates src="user" />
                <certificates src="system" />
            </trust-anchors>
        </debug-overrides>
    
        <base-config cleartextTrafficPermitted="true">
            <trust-anchors>
                <certificates src="system" />
                <certificates src="user" />
            </trust-anchors>
        </base-config>
    </network-security-config>

Copy

    <?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
    <manifest xmlns:android="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android"
        xmlns:tools="http://schemas.android.com/tools">
    
        <uses-permission android:name="android.permission.INTERNET" />
    
        <application
            android:networkSecurityConfig="@xml/network_security_config">
            <activity
                ...
            </activity>
        </application>
    
    </manifest>

Copy

    /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh

Copy

    Usage: /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh -m <mode> [options]
    
    Modes:
      all             Set proxy and install certificate
      proxy           Set proxy only
      revertProxy     Revert proxy settings only
      certificate     Install certificate only
    
    Required Options based on Mode:
      -m, --mode <mode>              : Operation mode (all, proxy, revertProxy, certificate)
      -i, --ip <ip_address>          : IP address (required for all, proxy, certificate)
      -p, --port <port_number>       : Port number (required for all, proxy, certificate)
      -c, --cert <path_to_cert.pem>  : Path to Proxyman certificate (required for all, certificate)
    
    Optional Options:
      --include-physical            : Include physical devices (default: only emulators)
      -h, --help                    : Show this help message

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh --mode all --ip <current_ip> --port <port> --cert <certificate_path>

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh all <current_ip> <port> <certificate_path>

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh --mode proxy --ip <current_ip> --port <port>

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh proxy <current_ip> <port> 

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh --mode revertProxy

Copy

    bash /Applications/Proxyman.app/Contents/Frameworks/ProxymanCore.framework/Resources/install_certificate_android_emulator.sh revertProxy
