# Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#proxyman-proxy-helper-tool)

Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

By default, Proxyman will try overriding your HTTP/HTTPS Proxy Config by using the [networksetup](https://www.unix.com/man-page/osx/8/networksetup/)
 Command-Line. However, the **networksetup** is a bottleneck during starting or quitting the app.

Proxyman offers a better solution: **Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool**, which is a [Privileged Helper Tool macOS](https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/documentation/Security/Conceptual/SecureCodingGuide/Articles/AccessControl.html#//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40002589-SW2)
 in order to override Network Proxy in **high performance**.[](https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/documentation/Security/Conceptual/SecureCodingGuide/Articles/AccessControl.html#//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40002589-SW2)

You can notice the performance difference by starting the app with or without the Proxy Setting Tool.

At the first launch, Proxyman will present the Popup to install the Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool. You can skip it and install it later in **Preference** -> **Advanced** Tab.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fz5NANcGQ78LwAeRx9Ykr%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202022-10-25%2520at%252010.11.32.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a4d3dfd-ad0f-49db-95a4-54061acd74f8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95a170f2&sv=2)

After the installation, you can find the Helper tool at `/Library/PrivilegedHelperTools/com.proxyman.NSProxy.HelperTool`

If Proxyman releases a new update for Proxy Setting Helper Tool, it requires installation again.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#require-user-permission-for-macos-13-ventura-or-later)

Require user Permission for macOS 13 Ventura or later

MacOS Ventura or later requires permission to work properly.

To grant the permission, please follow the steps:

1.  Open System Setting -> General -> Login Items
    
2.  Find Proxyman and Switch ON ✅
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F9nF5gGsEhfLDcQdRmHVl%252FScreenshot%25202022-11-20%2520at%252021.10.43.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d5d3c92-41eb-4e05-966e-cd20fcd004a1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=51eb22ed&sv=2)

Grant permission to Proxyman Helper Tool

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#guest-or-non-admin-users)

Guest or non-admin users

If you're a guest or non-admin user, the `networksetup` CLI would fail and could not change the HTTP/HTTPS Proxy config until you install the Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool.

Proxyman Proxy Helper Tool has privileged permission to override the proxy config for all kinds of users.

We highly recommend installing the Proxyman Helper Tool if you're a guest or non-admin user to make the UX smoother.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#uninstall-the-proxy-helper-tool)

Uninstall the Proxy Helper Tool

You can uninstall the Proxy Helper Tool in **Preference** -> **Advanced** Tab -> **Uninstall** Proxy Setting Tool or delete it directly at `/Library/PrivilegedHelperTools/com.proxyman.NSProxy.HelperTool`

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#install-the-proxy-helper-tool-by-command-line)

Install the Proxy Helper Tool by command line


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From macOS 4.12.0 or later, you can install the Helper Tool without GUI.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#changelog)

Changelog


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#version-1.6.0-proxyman-5.11.0-or-later)

Version 1.6.0 (Proxyman 5.11.0 or later)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Fixed: Proxyman can't restore the PAC URL when the app is closed
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#version-1.5.0)

**Version 1.5.0**

*   Fix the Security Vulnerability that Proxyman v1.5.0 or older (2019) can connect to the Helper Tool (v1.4.0) and override the system proxy without user consent. This fix will add some constraints to verify the incoming Connection. (The caller must be notarized by Apple, signed by Proxyman LLC Certificate, enabled Library Validation, and enabled Force Hard flag). (CVE-2023-45732)
    

📣 Credit to **Scott Leitch** from NCC Group.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#version-1.4.0)

**Version 1.4.0**

*   Comply with new macOS 13 Ventura Requirements for Helper Tool
    
*   Show App Icon & App Name on the Login-Items
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FKocgcP9YjaxeEiDqxj33%252F197530484-0f897b6f-7905-4d65-bdc3-86d2fc8abebe.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D256c80a1-6b41-4e48-844f-3e59f5146ae1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1792347a&sv=2)

Display correct Proxyman icon and App Name

On macOS Ventura, Helper Tools, Launch Daemon, and Launch Agent will be added to the Allow in the Background, even though Proxyman only runs on the Foreground.

There is an ongoing discussion on [Twitter](https://twitter.com/siracusa/status/1583914093437935616?s=46&t=C1XB91IkDFkG697Ab8T9Dg)
 that macOS should fix it.

After installing the 1.4.0, the Login Item might not be updated due to the cache layer of the Preference.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F7fUVML4Pct3p3YrRKm8a%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202022-10-25%2520at%252010.00.04.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2df5d008-0d39-4770-bce5-9e1e81af6b44&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=423dc11f&sv=2)

Invalid Cache

To fix it:

1.  Open Terminal app -> Run: `sfltool resetbtm`
    
2.  Restart the macOS
    
3.  Done
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#version-1.3.0)

**Version 1.3.0**

*   Remember and restore to your previous Proxy Setting.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/proxy-setting-tool#version-1.2.0)

Version 1.2.0:

*   Gracefully revert the HTTP Proxy Config if Proxyman is crashed.

# Bypass Proxy List | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-1.-bypass-proxy-list)

1\. Bypass Proxy List


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Bypass Proxy Lis helps developers to:

*   ✅ Define a list of domains that **never** go to the Proxyman Proxy Server
    
*   Ignore some noised traffic
    
*   Avoid SSL Error due to SSL Pinning when proxying to the Proxyman app.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-2.-how-to-use-it)

2\. How to use it?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Open the Bypass Proxy List in Tools Menu -> SSL Proxying List -> Bypass Proxy List
    
2.  Enter your list of domains (separated by Comma, support simple wildcard)
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FPXB4FYDowedIffXgRvi4%252FCleanShot%25202023-06-27%2520at%252008.28.08%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4de2503f-a327-45f7-ae0a-d1c87a5dcc6e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=39b4c3b7&sv=2)

Define a list of bypass proxy list

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-3.-how-does-it-work)

3\. How does it work?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  As soon as the Proxyman app is launched, Proxyman will override your system Bypass Proxy List with Proxyman List. You can find the system setting in System Setting -> Wi-Fi -> Your Wifi hotspot -> Details… -> Proxy -> Bypass Proxy List
    
2.  When the app is closed -> Proxyman will revert to your original setting.
    

[PreviousSSL Proxying](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/ssl-proxying)
[NextImport / Export](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. Bypass Proxy List](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-1.-bypass-proxy-list)
    
*   [2\. How to use it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-2.-how-to-use-it)
    
*   [3\. How does it work?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/bypass-proxy-list#id-3.-how-does-it-work)

# Horizontal/Vertical/Window Layout | Proxyman

It's possible to change the UI layout of the Request and Response Panels to optimize your space to render the content.

*   **Detachable Window**: Bring Request and Response to a seperated Windows
    
*   **Vertical**: Request and Response Panel is in Vertical Mode
    
*   **Horizontal**: Request and Response Panel is in Horizontal Mode
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5kgZfgX_GZuzjAbAQT%252F-M5khQdFnInkcHQX-Ci_%252F02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6ff8a61-f333-4b80-91d8-24c98d3bd60d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b92a3095&sv=2)

Shortcut

Description

⇧**⌘ + Up Arrow**

Detachable Window

⇧**⌘ + Left Arrow**

Toggle Left Panel

⇧**⌘ + Right Arrow**

Vertical Mode

⇧**⌘ + Down Arrow**

Horizontal Mode

[PreviousMultiple Tabs](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/multiple-tabs)
[NextCopy as](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/copy-as)

Last updated 5 years ago

# Copy as | Proxyman

Proxyman offers various Copy functions from Right-click menu Context:

*   **Copy URL**: Copy URL of the selected flow.
    
*   **Copy cURL**: Generate cURL command, which includes headers, cookies, query, and body.
    
*   **Copy Cell Value**: Copy a string value of the right-clicked cell
    
*   **Copy as**: Cookies, Header, Body from Request and Response.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-Mi5Obfjpop55gBQYfpT%252F-Mi5OpUlB_gDXH3xmEtf%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-08-27%2520at%252013.58.35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5736a09a-12c5-41ba-9190-1d9e37f8002e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98b25826&sv=2)

Copy selected requests

You can opt-out the `--proxy` flag from cURL command from Preference -> Advanced -> Uncheck "Include HTTP Proxy config in cURL"

**⌘C:** Copy the URL

⇧**⌘C:** Copy as **cURL**

[PreviousHorizontal/Vertical/Window Layout](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/horizontal-vertical-layout)
[NextCustom Previewer Tab](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab)

Last updated 4 years ago

# Filter JSON Response | Proxyman

You can quickly filter the JSON Response with the following approach:

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-1.-filter-on-json-previewer)

1\. Filter on JSON Previewer

*   **⌘F** to trigger the Filter
    
*   Support Regex
    
*   Support Jump Next
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MIxxav7aI2mJ6cNqZrq%252F-MIxxuqk-fVjjHSX9dcr%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-06_at_19_47_47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dad576252-9751-43cd-87a9-d3ae06fb71f2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a4bac79&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-2.-jsonpath)

2\. JSONPath

Proxyman supports [JSONPath](https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath#path-examples)
 for quickly querying the data in JSON Document.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MfzvKgHrrVOB_SexW44%252F-MfzvapgK9JWsYTJn6dt%252FScreen_Shot_2021-08-01_at_10_29_23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8aedc2a1-3dad-478d-8c5e-442e2caf0a2c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6dd9ed9a&sv=2)

Please check out JSONPath documentation.

[JSONPath](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-3.-keypaths)

3\. KeyPaths

*   Support Key Paths filter on JSON Tree View mode
    
*   Search specifically the children keys
    

Syntax example:

*   **posts\[1\].maker\[2\]**: Go from Root -> Get item at index 1 of the Posts array -> Get the index 3 items of Makers array and filter out
    
*   **users.name**: Get the name value of the "users" dictionary
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MIxxav7aI2mJ6cNqZrq%252F-MIxy5sNhUXUbfvyiijX%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-06_at_19_30_35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De80edbe7-da3d-497b-acfa-130944b57daf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=31900698&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-4.-all-keys-or-all-values)

4\. All Keys or All Values

*   Show all nodes that the key or value contains the search text
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MIxyS6P3poAOWR9J7RQ%252F-MIxzB4KkDq13VJqL13z%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-10-06%2520at%252014.21.26.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7a3bef8a-0f16-4d52-ba84-8bc1632edbe0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcca4f19&sv=2)

[PreviousRegex (Regular Expression)](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex)
[NextHighlight by Color and Add Comment](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/highlight-by-color-and-add-comment)

Last updated 4 years ago

*   [1\. Filter on JSON Previewer](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-1.-filter-on-json-previewer)
    
*   [2\. JSONPath](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response#id-2.-jsonpath)

# Content Filter | Proxyman

Proxyman offers the Primary and Secondary Filters to quickly filter out the Requests or Responses you're looking for.

**⌘F: Open** Filter Bar quickly

**ESC** to close the Filter Bar

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MWPWuYgIo6i6gTJSUIl%252F-MWPYdeG67U8YQg8xfyU%252FScreen_Shot_2021-03-22_at_22_29_07.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debd757b9-16c6-4362-9c50-7825716bc1ee&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9bf27949&sv=2)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MMIpB1h4e4aRQJKKSDY%252F-MMIpSwCM9NRjZsf8y-r%252FCleanShot%25202020-11-17%2520at%252008.31.52%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D57846212-6b13-4b14-bb05-480b4ad6b915&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bfe6f6fa&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#primary-filter)

Primary Filter:

Filter

Description

All

All Requests and Responses

HTTP

Only HTTP

HTTPS

Only HTTPS

WebSocket

Only WebSocket and Secure WebSocket

JSON

Content-Type is application/json or JSON contents

XML

Only XML

Form

Only Form Body in Request / Response

JS

Only JavaScript content

CSS

Only CSS content

Document

Documents content: HTML, ...

Media

Image contents: PNG, JPG, GIF, ...

Other

Other contents which no matching with the above.

Font

All font family

GraphQL

GraphQL Request (has suffix `/graphQL`)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#status-filters)

Status Filters:

Filter

Description

1xx

Status Code from 100-200

2xx

Status Code from 200-300

3xx

Status Code from 300-400

4xx

Status Code from 400-500

5xx

Status Code from 500

Hold CMD key and Click to select multiple Types

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#secondary-filter)

Secondary Filter:

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#content)

Content:

*   URL
    
*   Query String
    
*   Request Header
    
*   Response Header
    
*   Method
    
*   Status Code
    
*   Comment
    
*   Color
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#matching)

Matching:

*   Contains
    
*   Not Contains
    
*   Start With
    
*   End With
    
*   Equal
    
*   Not Equal
    
*   Regex
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/content-filter#header-query-auth-form-filter)

Header, Query, Auth, Form Filter

From Proxyman 2.34.0+, we can quickly filter the Header, Query, Auth, Form from the selected Request and Response.

1.  Click on the view (e.g. Header of the Request)
    
2.  Use Hotkey: CMD + F or Right-Click -> Show Filter to open the filter
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FGPUIjUQipzWKwvRAl8bq%252FScreen_Shot_2021-10-14_at_22_59_20.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D05a7c277-e8b5-4a76-8a1f-eaeb5f1de1a2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bcfb84b6&sv=2)

# Request / Response Previewer | Proxyman

After installing the [Certificate](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)
 and enable [HTTP Response](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/ssl-proxying)
 on domains or clients, your network traffic would show up immediately inside the Proxyman window, separated into three main areas:

*   The Source List on the left panel
    
*   The Flow List on the middle panel
    
*   The Flow Content on the right panel
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5k_8UnCbVU-a0Ksr1u%252F-M5kcU0AOTr014EyiUPT%252F01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9bce65ca-8c22-433e-902b-a309977ba9e2&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba1e3586&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#body-content-previewer)

Body Content Previewer

Depend on what the content of the Request or Response is: Proxyman will automatically show in separate tabs:

*   **Header**: All headers (key-value table)
    
*   **Cookies**: **Cookie** key in the header
    
*   **Set-Cookie** for the Set-Cookie Header in the Response
    
*   **Auth**: **Authentication** key in the header
    
*   **Body**: The body of the message: Proxyman automatically formats and beautifies the body content depends on the **Content-Type,** such as JSON, PNG, GIF, Raw Data, ...
    
*   **Query**: If the request has a query, all queries are presented.
    
*   **Raw**: The RAW HTTP message.
    
*   Protobuf Message
    
*   MessagePack
    
*   Multipart/form-data
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#custom-previewer-tab)

Custom Previewer Tab

It's possible to customize which Previewer Tab you would like to see

*   Custom tabs will persistent on the Request/Response Panel
    
*   Attempt to decode and beautify the content
    

[Custom Previewer Tab](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-Md01ISVIn5N9gt1kT_C%252F-Md01URMXqWeaY7AsRN1%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-06-25%2520at%252009.39.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0e66b6bc-cb2c-49bd-860f-ca056224914d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=28654dab&sv=2)

Custom Previewer Tab

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#layout-mode)

Layout mode

There are two way to order the Request / Response Panel: Vertical or Horizontal layout

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-LmSUd_OpdDpUrjpkX-6%252F-LmSVFKeUuNPwG6HpV-Y%252Fhttp_response_vertical.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6d53954-50df-450a-af52-af459f5661c6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b3ebcfe2&sv=2)

Request/ Response Panel

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5k_8UnCbVU-a0Ksr1u%252F-M5kdG7Ych9_JbU82Mm7%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252016.21.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D628d3d65-a04b-4293-8736-694b1eb81a81&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9aa25544&sv=2)

Previewer in Horizontal Layout

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5k_8UnCbVU-a0Ksr1u%252F-M5kdOeUJerSyTDQLo45%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252016.21.55.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82117838-42e8-47f1-b9de-30291225395e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b8614116&sv=2)

Previewer in Vertical layout

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#customize-workspace)

Customize Workspace

You can use custom layout buttons on the top right corner of the app to display content as your preference

1.  Collapse/Expand Source List Panel
    
2.  Open Request/ Response Panel in new window
    
3.  Display Request/Response Panel in Horizontal layout
    
4.  Display Request/Response Panel in Vertical layout
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5kgZfgX_GZuzjAbAQT%252F-M5khQdFnInkcHQX-Ci_%252F02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df6ff8a61-f333-4b80-91d8-24c98d3bd60d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b92a3095&sv=2)

Shortcuts

 blog

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#body-previewer)

**Body Previewer**

Body previewer automatically beautifies the content as well as offering handy minor features:

*   **Tree View**: Represent the JSON in Tree View mode
    
*   **Hex**: Show the body in Hex format
    
*   **Export only body**: Able to export your body content to file. Suitable for Raw Data or binary data
    
*   **Open With**: You can open the Body content with your favorite Editor. **Sublime Text** is mime 😍
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-LmSXcp2h6D33De4N0wo%252F-LmSXeS1vqgVfomWgdCG%252Fbody_previewer.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8753aa59-aaf1-4000-aed2-54ce2a45b709&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=989221ba&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/request-response-viewer#json-tree-view-mode)

JSON Tree View mode

Proxyman supports native JSON Tree View mode, which displays a JSON Body. It allows the developer to:

*   Search JSON by [JSON Path](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths)
    
*   Copy JSON Node like Google Developer Tool does.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FxD1Lpl6PBL1gU4GwVpWo%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-10-15%2520at%252016.14.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db22d8a79-401a-4609-b17b-adca36609cd4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=46698bbc&sv=2)

# Custom Previewer Tab | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can customize the Custom Previewer Tabs, which always render one format at once time.

This handy tool might help you to fix the following issues:

*   Format the BODY as **JSON**, but the Content-Type isn't `application/json`
    
*   Format the body as **Protobuf**, but the Content-Type isn't `application/x-protobuf`
    
*   Render HTML Page on the Web View
    
*   **Beautify** the minified files (HTML, CSS, JS)
    
*   Multipart/form-data
    
*   Try to format the body as the selected type regardless of the `Content-Type`
    
*   Convert MessagePack (msgpack) to JSON
    
*   [Code Generator](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/code-generator)
     to Swift, Node, Javascript, cURL, ...
    
*   GraphQL Query Prettier
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FQS5DmASN352ZCEhDybUH%252FScreenshot%25202024-06-27%2520at%252015.01.33.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db852b3ea-d443-41c7-98f7-7d43e2c29b1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76e1700a&sv=2)

Select Custom Tabs for Request / Response Panel

The selected custom tabs will be appended to the right side of the Request or Response view

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F8Si69osmNYVI79U5igeE%252FCleanShot%25202024-06-27%2520at%252015.04.11%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D24b4d6d6-546f-4636-bec9-4236b3886131&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=6cbd8a5e&sv=2)

Display Custom Tabs

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab#id-2.-how-to-use-it)

2\. How to use it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can either access the Custom Previewer Window:

1.  Click on the "+" button on the Request/Response bar or (from the Tools Menu -> Custom Previewer Tab...)
    
2.  Click the checkbox to show/hide your custom Tab
    
3.  The New Tab will appear on the Request or Response Panel ✅
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab#id-2.1-server-sent-events-and-openai-tabs)

2.1 Server-Sent Events and OpenAI Tabs

From Proxyman 5.22.0 or later, Proxyman supports

*   Server-Sent Events from OpenAI endpoints: Auto prettify the inline JSON of the data event
    
*   OpenAI Tab: Auto accumulate the content and show the final result, similar to the output of your chat view.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Ff91nElaK93AiZfFIA9F5%252F1.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70d6c8e1-96a5-4845-9248-8a33197381b6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=548fbe&sv=2)

Capture OpenAI Endpoints

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab#id-3.-advance-create-a-custom-tab-with-the-scripting-tool)

3\. ⚡️ Advance: Create a custom Tab with the Scripting Tool


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ✅ Show your own data on your tab
    
*   It is useful if you want to decode your Body or display a partial body to your custom tab
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-previewer-tab#how-to-use)

How to use:

1.  the Click on the "+" button on the Request/Response bar or (from the Tools Menu -> Custom Previewer Tab...)
    
2.  Select the \`Add Custom Tab\` button
    
3.  Select the Request / Response panel and set a name for your tab
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F5n0TQEJYkZsvnLWgAFAk%252FScreenshot%25202024-06-27%2520at%252015.01.51.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab0a5dc7-09d7-4347-810d-c896df4ee25b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2206982d&sv=2)

1.  Click on the "..." button to show the Javascript Code
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F126T05MtmP31imNqEufD%252F343035426-24d2901d-10e3-4fa0-a472-579df7385358.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63eba6be-1927-4355-9c0b-8be2cf07b91b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3ea3aa8&sv=2)

Show the Javascript Code

1.  Tools -> Scripting -> Add new Rule -> Use this code to display your own data
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F53QsgUDH9BoykmkyvvJB%252F343035431-1a336092-5c50-4e23-afbb-9a41f9679bb9.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D456de21a-499a-44c8-99d5-2bd2245e7722&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7fbd8fd0&sv=2)

Write your code to display data

1.  Done
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FQluL2BFeo0yziUnxuWGC%252F343035436-dc7e6346-9ac6-4601-b07a-8294de2c4a02.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D513c916e-4071-4881-b84c-672fa2ef6664&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=11f9dfd0&sv=2)

Display your data on a new tab

# JQ | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jq#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   jq is like sed for JSON data - you can use it to slice and filter and map and transform structured data with the same ease that sed, awk, grep and friends let you play with text.
    
*   Available on Proxyman 5.24.0 or later
    

*   jq Filter is only available in the JSON Tab. On the Request/Response Tool bar -> Click on the + button -> Select JSON in the Request or Response. A new JSON Tab will be added.
    

![use jq to filter JSON Body](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEdE7E1m2tEj7mNEiB4Tf%252F481323588-7ae7cb0a-ca66-4199-a16d-e171960a9814.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da2dacd3b-74ec-4853-aa3b-ec19464fc6a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a5d728ad&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jq#id-2.-syntax)

2\. Syntax


----------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Please refer the [jq Manual Page](https://jqlang.org/manual/#basic-filters)
     to understand how to use the jq
    

[PreviousJSONPath](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths)
[NextCustomize Toolbar](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/customize-toolbar)

Last updated 3 months ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jq#id-1.-whats-it)

# Highlight by Color and Add Comment | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/highlight-by-color-and-add-comment#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can

*   **Highlight** a single or group of Request with pre-defined **colors** (Red, Yellow, Green, Blue, Purple, Gray)
    
*   Add ~Strikethrough~
    
*   Add Comment
    
*   Filter by Color or Comment (CMD+F)
    
*   Export with Color and Comment (Only Support Proxyma Log format)
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MLqzpCGC7fhsZP0KuAM%252F-MLr0L3vQE6h4Y24t9Ut%252Fhighligh_by_colors.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2a440e68-7d9f-4c58-82ad-0177079f4de9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=90b80d2d&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/highlight-by-color-and-add-comment#id-2.-benefit)

2\. Benefit?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Easily mark your failed, succeed request/response with eye-catching colors
    
*   Add Comments during development.
    
*   Share it with your colleague (Color and Comment)
    
*   Easily filter out the request/response by Color or Commend
    

3\. Shortcuts?

Proxyman supports many shortcuts to help you highlight or add comments quickly.

Shotcut

Purpose

⌘1

Highlight with Red Color

⌘2

Highlight with Yellow Color

⌘3

Highlight with Green Color

⌘4

Highlight with Blue Color

⌘5

Highlight with Purple Color

⌘6

Highlight with Gray Color

⌘0

Reset All

⌘/

Add Strikethrough style

⌘M

Add Comment to selected requests

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MLqzpCGC7fhsZP0KuAM%252F-MLr1rRQmtk5bQSaoSJ2%252Fshortcut.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6bec325c-eb29-4ec8-b966-c890257f76f6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1444e949&sv=2)

[PreviousFilter JSON Response](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response)
[NextImport / Export Settings](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings)

Last updated 5 years ago

# Localization | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/localization#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Proxyman supports localization, which affect all UI of the app. The following list is a current langauges:

*   English (Default)
    
*   Chinese - Simplified
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/localization#id-2.-how-to-override-the-app-language)

2\. How to override the app language?

By default, Proxyman will respect the current System Language. To override it, please:

*   System Preference -> Language & Region -> Select Apps Tab -> Add Proxyman app -> Click the + button -> Select Proxyman app and English.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/localization#id-3.-improve-localization)

3\. Improve localization?

If you've encountered a poor translation in your languages, please help us a hand at [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/proxyman-localization](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/proxyman-localization)

[PreviousCustomize Toolbar](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/customize-toolbar)
[NextQuick Preview](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/quick-preview)

Last updated 3 years ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/localization#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. How to override the app language?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/localization#id-2.-how-to-override-the-app-language)

# Quick Preview | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/quick-preview#id-1.-what-is-it)

1\. What is it?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The quick view can help you to quick preview the selected in any place of the app.

*   Beautify inline JSON
    
*   Decode Base64 String
    
*   Display key&value as a table
    
*   Decode JWT Token
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEvRMopxPmFDnYysOlZ4w%252FCleanShot%25202023-03-22%2520at%252015.26.10%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D912ab226-8ed0-4616-bc9b-4677e6ba5465&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=186758fe&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/quick-preview#id-2.-how-to-use-it)

2\. How to use it?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Select any text on the app, e.g Body Tab, Raw Tab, etc
    
2.  Right Click to show the menu context
    
3.  Select Text Selection View as Mode
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FAXE2yKuaUrzEXZyANZ9y%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-22%2520at%252015.19.32.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58b39c89-50e4-4f98-a37f-047bc622a281&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=178c0cfd&sv=2)

Quick View on the Raw Tab

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FYUAjfacWA13e2rHYRRQt%252FScreenshot%25202023-03-22%2520at%252015.19.59.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ec93819-f94c-4bac-a055-c70171e9fdb6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=371a3e84&sv=2)

# Regex (Regular Expression) | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From the 2.3.0 version, Proxyman supports **Wildcard** and **Regex** (Match a whole word) when you define matching rules for all available tools:

*   Map Local
    
*   Map Remote
    
*   Block & Allow List
    
*   Breakpoints
    
*   Protocol Buffers (Protobuf)
    
*   Reverse Proxy
    
*   Network Throttling
    
*   ...
    

It's a handy tool to help you exactly define which requests should trigger the tool.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MC_ByEFfDEzSzI1C7Zz%252F-MC_DZnVSPfddI4tnDir%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-07-19%2520at%252010.17.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df468fd18-608d-4841-9c4b-fa47236b4f24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abb8c04e&sv=2)

Match a request by Wildcard or Regex

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-2.-test-your-url-new-feature)

2\. Test your URL (New feature 🎉)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman v4.8.0, you can quickly test your Rule (Wildcard / Regex).

*   You can quickly test & play around with your Wildcard/Regex
    
*   **Save time**: You don't need to go back and forth to check your URL.
    
*   Less error-prone.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FCV72j0RaTiGL2BkCUv0l%252FCleanShot%25202023-05-09%2520at%252009.54.22%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbf4a216a-476b-4cb1-acbd-17f6db58919c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=81b3e9a3&sv=2)

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#how-to-use-it)

How to use it?

1.  Open any debugging tools (Breakpoint, Map Local, ...) -> Create a new rule
    
2.  Click on the "Test your Rule" underline button -> New Window is opened.
    
3.  Add your Rule and URLs you'd like to check
    

*   ✅ Matched: Your URL is matched with your rule.
    
*   ⚠️ Not Matched: Your URL doesn't match your rule. You might rewrite your wildcard/Regex rule.
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-3.-wildcard)

3\. Wildcard


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman supports simple Wildcard characters, which include `*` and `?`

Wildcard

Purpose

`*`

The asterisk in a wildcard matches any character zero or more times.

`?`

A question mark matches a single character once.

For instance:

*   http://proxyman.io/v1/\*
    
*   https://myserver.com/v?/\*
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-4.-regex)

4\. Regex


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman also supports Regex.

*   Make sure your regex is **matching a whole URL**.
    
*   **Partial Matching** is considered as not matching.
    
*   Make sure you **escape characters** properly: Splash (/), full-stop (.), etc.
    

For instance:

Regex

Matched URL Examples

https:\\/\\/proxyman\\.io.\*

https://proxyman.io https://proxyman.io/v1/data?id=123 https://proxyman.io/pricing

^(http|https):\\/\\/www\\.google\\.com.\*

http://www.google.com http://www.google.com/user?id=proxyman https://www.google.com

^(http|https)?:\\/\\/www\\.google\\.com\\/v\[0-9\]?\\/build\\?query=proxyman

http://www.google.com/v1/build?query=proxyman www.google.com/v2/build?query=proxyman

You can use [https://regex101.com/](https://regex101.com/)
 to verify your Regex that matches the whole text.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FNUJWU7lPdcdGjhR9f6ye%252F1.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D681d1a5d-e0a8-42a1-8aa5-8df6fb2adb4e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8b0737f2&sv=2)

Make sure your Regex matches whole words

Please check the [**Regex** **Metacharacters, Operator and Flag**](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/foundation/nsregularexpression#1965590)
 from Apple Developer Documents to know which one is supported.

Check [https://regex101.com](https://regex101.com/)
 and make sure your Regex is full-matching with the given URL

*   Select Regex when creating rules
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MC_ByEFfDEzSzI1C7Zz%252F-MC_GHgRHPy8AUEjilO4%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-07-19%2520at%252010.17.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc380ce78-9b3f-4ee8-be9e-6e6ee31d3e76&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9e0640b&sv=2)

With regular expressions the meaning of `?` and `*` is different from that of wildcards. The equivalent of wildcard `?` is the regex `.` and the equivalent of wildcard `*` is the regex `.*`

[PreviousCustom Header Column](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column)
[NextFilter JSON Response](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/filter-json-response)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. Test your URL (New feature 🎉)](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-2.-test-your-url-new-feature)
    
*   [3\. Wildcard](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex#id-3.-wildcard)

# Custom Header Column | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Custom Header Column feature allows you to customize the column that displays on the main Table View. It's similar to Custom Header Column from [Google Chrome Dev Tools](https://developers.google.com/web/tools/chrome-devtools/network/reference#custom-columns)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column#id-2.-benefit)

2\. Benefit

*   Define a Header from Request/Response and show it on the table.
    
*   **Easier to distinguish each request/response if they have the same URL, but different Headers**
    
*   Support resize/sorting/reorder columns
    
*   Remember the previous state and restore it for the future session.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column#id-3.-how-to-use-it)

3\. How to use it?

You can open **Tool Menu** -> **Custom Header Column**

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MVepXPi2YNzkeoVqOWB%252F-MVesDI6M8IiS5UtE1-9%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-03-13%2520at%252016.15.45.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4506d8ac-3d57-4d8a-962a-45a4761abc1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=98548812&sv=2)

Custom your header column

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MVepXPi2YNzkeoVqOWB%252F-MVerXncCd4zbCjZz_zd%252FScreen_Shot_2021-03-13_at_16_08_14.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2acbe179-0905-4a17-a7dc-305bd4652741&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3a9ab906&sv=2)

It will display on the main Table View

If you need to manage the default columns, please right-click on the Column Header.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MVepXPi2YNzkeoVqOWB%252F-MVetSwMrJ3MJXUAjQKW%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-03-13%2520at%252016.21.39.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De258c27e-d247-40aa-99e5-42f3ea980137&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9e36359e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column#graphql-query-column)

**GraphQL Query Column**

Custom Header Column would extract and display the query name for GraphQL Request.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MVepXPi2YNzkeoVqOWB%252F-MVetX1HGlYXY9NQS7A3%252FScreen_Shot_2021-03-13_at_16_20_42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7f16b9c-d200-4742-b158-db9f23cdd42b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9eb2898&sv=2)

# Import / Export Settings | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings#id-1.-import-settings)

1\. Import Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 2.26.0, the developer can import the Tools Settings from other colleagues who are using **Proxyman** or **Charles Proxy**.

To import settings, please go to Tools -> Import Settings -> From Proxyman / Charles Proxy -> Select the tools you would like to import

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M_s4PMn2IXBt6drz9PV%252F-M_s5AZDJrJ7HW4n81LP%252FScreen_Shot_2021-05-17_at_09_11_44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6eb389ba-60a1-4754-a81d-3480eccf3e97&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cc9057c4&sv=2)

The following list will describe what tools that you can import:

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings#proxyman)

Proxyman

*   SSL Proxying List
    
*   Block List
    
*   White List
    
*   Map Local
    
*   Map Remote
    
*   Breakpoint
    
*   Network Condition
    
*   Scripting
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings#charles-proxy)

Charles Proxy

*   SSL Proxying List
    
*   Block List
    
*   White List
    
*   Map Local
    
*   Map Remote
    
*   Breakpoint
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings#id-2.-export-settings)

2\. Export Settings


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can also export the Tools Settings then sharing to your colleagues.

1.  Open the tool you would like to export
    
2.  Select Rules
    
3.  Right Click -> Export Setting
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M_s4PMn2IXBt6drz9PV%252F-M_s6EMoJZUREXqeKusD%252FScreen_Shot_2021-05-17_at_09_16_41.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d5c4d29-a5a9-4527-b603-d4bd95bb8775&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5765da0&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/import-export-settings#id-3.-open-charles-proxy-log-file-.chls)

3\. Open Charles Proxy Log File (\*.chls)


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman supports open Charles Proxy Log file, which is exported from Charles Proxy app. Please check out the Charles Proxy Converter.

[Charles Proxy Converter](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/charles-proxy-converter)

# Command Palette | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/command-palette#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Introduce a global Command Palette that helps developers:

*   Quickly search Debugging Tools
    
*   Toggle Debugging Tools
    
*   Open a new Guideline for iOS, Simulator, Android, and Emulators
    
*   Pin your most used action
    

![Proxyman with Command Palette](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FjMixkAfufiUoaYhVtXK4%252FScreenshot%25202025-10-03%2520at%252020.39.57.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70f3aa13-e8d0-4c57-8485-bd574802b4de&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8672b511&sv=2)

Use ⌘⇧P to open the Command Palette Windows

Command Palette is available on Proxyman macOS 5.26.0 or later

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/command-palette#id-2.-missing-your-shortcut)

2\. Missing your shortcut?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Map Local (File) | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Map Local Tool enables you to use the content of local files as an HTTP Response to your requests.

You can do Map Local for **GraphQL** with the Scripting Tool ([Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#map-local-with-graphql)
)

You can combine **Map Local with Breakpoint** to modify the content on the fly (2.16.0+)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-2.-benefits)

2\. Benefits


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Define a Response with Status Code, Headers, and Body -> Mock to a given Request -> Easily to test some edge cases without waiting for the server's update.
    
*   **Mock Fake API with a local File**: It's useful for developers to try out the testing APIs that are not in production.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MgdA6B5loIY55XPs0WC%252F-MgdAvRMcpn98kCytuZk%252FScreen_Shot_2021-08-09_at_11_28_40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D33cc4302-c682-46c5-8717-83f0e67d7fb7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=110c28ea&sv=2)

Define Status Code, Headers and Body

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-an-http-message)

With an HTTP Message

1.  Right Click on your request on the main table -> Tools -> Map Local -> Proxyman will automatically create a new rules with a current Response
    
2.  Feel free to change the Status Code, Headers and the JSON Body
    
3.  Done
    
4.  Re-sent your request -> New Response is mapped.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-a-local-file)

With a Local File

*   Click on the `Select Local File` button and select any files. Supports: Text, JSON, Binary, Image
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-less-than-file_url-greater-than-flag)

With <FILE\_URL> flag

*   It's useful to map to a given file and able to provide the Status Code and Response Headers.
    
*   Work with JSON, Text, Binary, Image etc
    
*   Make sure to provide `Content-Type` header, so your client can work properly
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-2.-how-to-use)

2\. How to use


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  Right-click on the Request (which already has a Response) -> Tools -> Map Local. Proxyman will create a rule with the current Response Body (The file is stored in your Desktop folder)
    
2.  We can directly change the Response body.
    
3.  Make a request and observe the new Response Body.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FAFwzclnJSuLiNFYdOdrm%252FScreen_Shot_2022-09-23_at_13_23_11.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daebf9100-157a-40de-af45-a428c978cf7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=36798e9b&sv=2)

Create a Map Local with curernt Response

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-3.-map-local-with-graphql-requests)

3\. Map Local with GraphQL Requests


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 2.27.0+, Map Local can work with GraphQL Request by a specific QueryName. Please check out the following GraphQL Document.

[GraphQL](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-4.-map-local-with-scripting-tool)

4\. Map Local with Scripting Tool ✅


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you would like to do Map Local with **complicated rules,** you might check out [Scripting](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#1-whats-it)
 since it's easier to achieve the same result.

Please check out these [Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#2-common-on-request-and-response)
 to understand how to map a local file with Javascript Code.

[PreviousBreakpoint Templates](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates)
[NextMap Local (Directory)](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local-directory)

*   [2\. Benefits](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-2.-benefits)
    
*   [With an HTTP Message](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-an-http-message)
    
*   [With a Local File](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-a-local-file)
    
*   [With <FILE\_URL> flag](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#with-less-than-file_url-greater-than-flag)
    
*   [2\. How to use](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-2.-how-to-use)
    
*   [3\. Map Local with GraphQL Requests](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-3.-map-local-with-graphql-requests)
    
*   [4\. Map Local with Scripting Tool ✅](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-local#id-4.-map-local-with-scripting-tool)
    

Copy

    HTTP/1.1 200 OK
    Content-Type: application/json
    
    <FILE_URL="~/Desktop/myjson.json">

# Breakpoint | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Breakpoint is a handy tool to help developers to edit the content of the Request and Response **on the fly**.

It's possible to set a breakpoint on both **Request** or **Response.**

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MEVxm7C1KsUVgql_NPM%252F-MEVyVnIP9VAXgkb-LUN%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-08-12%2520at%252011.39.46.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff9f8d86-60e6-4130-a83a-2da8324842e8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1dcf847&sv=2)

If you're using [Atlantis Framework](https://docs.proxyman.com/atlantis/atlantis-for-ios)
, you could not use Breakpoint. Please consider using a normal proxy.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-2.-main-features)

2\. Main features

Breakpoint tool allows the developer to stop an ongoing Request or incoming Response to modify its data.

*   Modify the Request URL, including the Scheme, Host, Path, Port, HTTP Method (Available on Proxyman 2.35.4+)
    
*   Modify HTTP Headers of Request/Response
    
*   Modify Query or Form entry from Requests.
    
*   Modify Authorization/Cookie/Set-Cookie Headers.
    
*   Modify HTTP Body of Request/Response
    
*   Change Response HTTP Status Code.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MhvV4r0O2ZZtJx7eDhO%252F-MhvVZiTBRRVnS8Z50yB%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202021-08-25%2520at%252011.12.06.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30144dc0-8a03-41a9-acf5-aa6fc49bd699&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2c2ddbe7&sv=2)

Breakpoint on Response

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FibeqdjhWzlVYHcrfDIUt%252FScreen_Shot_2021-12-20_at_15_06_05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D80446083-949b-4d70-ba48-6fa6ebccaccf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4a0c1d39&sv=2)

Breakpoint on the Request URL (Scheme, Host, Port, Path and Query)

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#breakpoint-actions)

Breakpoint Actions

Action

Meaning

Cancel

Cancel a breakpoint and continue the Request/Response

Abort

Abort the connection and return 503 status code

Execute

Make a request/response with a new change

Check out Breakpoint Tutorial: [Breakpoint to intercept and edit the requests/response on iOS app](https://proxyman.io/blog/2019/09/Use-Breakpoint-to-intercept-and-edit-request-response-on-iOS-app.html)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-3.-breakpoint-with-raw-message)

3\. Breakpoint with Raw Message

From build 3.1.0, we can modify the Request / Response by using the Raw Message.

\[WIP\]

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-4.-breakpoint-by-the-scripting-tool)

4\. Breakpoint by the Scripting Tool ✅

If you would like to do Breakpoint in an Automatic way, you should use the [Scripting](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#1-whats-it)
 tools, which you can achieve the same result that Breakpoint can do, but in a flexible way by writing Javascript Code.

Please check out this [Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#2-common-on-request-and-response)
 to understand how to use Scripting for Breakpoint.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-5.-breakpoint-with-graphql-requests)

5\. Breakpoint with GraphQL Requests

From Proxyman 2.27.0+, Breakpoint can work with GraphQL Request by a specific QueryName. Please check out the following GraphQL Document.

[GraphQL](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-6.-how-to-use)

6\. How to use

You can simply create a Breakpoint rule by:

1.  Right-Click on the Request -> Tools -> Breakpoint
    
2.  Proxyman will open a Breakpoint Window and fill the Matching Rule.
    
3.  Select Breakpoint on Request or Response or both.
    
4.  Click Add to create a rule.
    
5.  Try sending a Request again -> Proxyman will open a Breakpoint and you can modify the data.
    
6.  Click on the Execute Button to send a request/response.
    

[PreviousNo Caching](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching)
[NextBreakpoint Templates](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [2\. Main features](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#id-2.-main-features)

# Compose new Request | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

"Compose new Request" tool is a handy tool to help developers:

*   Compose an HTTP/HTTPS Request and send it to your service. It's similar to Paw, Insomnia, and Postman.
    
*   Quickly test your APIs without depending on your app client.
    
*   Support Header, Query, URL, Form, JSON Body
    
*   Support Raw Message
    
*   Support multipart body
    
*   Preset template: Empty Request, GET Request, Post Request with JSON or Form.
    

You can reuse your request data for new requests. Please check out the [Edit & Repeat](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/edit-and-repeat)
 page.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FKMaeS7lqansj0MX2Y8wK%252FScreenshot%25202025-09-05%2520at%252021.01.54.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc84e09d2-a3c7-46e1-b9d3-25566bad8a1c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1916e6df&sv=2)

Make a HTTPS Requests with Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-2.-how-to-use)

2\. How to use


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can open the tool by either:

*   Click on the Compose button on the main navigation bar
    
*   Tools -> Compose
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FIGNPhi6gMvEOZYunIvUA%252FScreen_Shot_2022-06-23_at_15_03_44.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D260f92a7-78d7-4790-a437-31f47a343937&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c5962425&sv=2)

Open the Compose Tool

1.  Enter the URL
    
2.  Select HTTP Method
    
3.  Modify the Header, Param, Body, Raw Message
    
4.  Click the Send button.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FiEGZEumelhi9RAkxfPAH%252FScreen_Shot_2022-06-23_at_15_07_35.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dac87cc51-3849-4aff-9da5-64814d6ffc6c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=138cbd8a&sv=2)

Compose JSON Body

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FvEQeGrMfgGXlcz8vpUIQ%252FScreen_Shot_2022-06-23_at_15_08_10.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D434a10dd-2b53-45ee-81e0-d1e69ebc513f&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=f1e17b57&sv=2)

Using Raw Message

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-3.-template)

3\. Template


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman also supports a few request templates.

*   GET with Query
    
*   Post with JSON
    
*   Post with Form
    
*   Post with multiparts
    
*   Import from cURL
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FwNaAyGBvUGZJ1YCA2Kcf%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-01%2520at%252010.45.59%25E2%2580%25AFPM.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dee860dd3-8095-40d7-92fc-2b282d9a1c77&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ab97b08a&sv=2)

Use preset template

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-4.-import-from-curl)

4\. Import from cURL


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

You can import your cURL, which you can copy from a Network Tab in Google Chrome and make a request with the Compose Tool.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FbUYslRNNBCc6EtHDTHLZ%252FScreenshot%25202025-02-01%2520at%252010.42.21%25E2%2580%25AFPM.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Deadf666f-03e2-4957-8bc7-81fa3831da4d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9354dbd2&sv=2)

import cURL

You can simply paste your cURL to the URL Text View, Proxyman will tries to parse your cURL

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-5.-history-request)

5\. History Request


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman macOS 5.24.0, Proxyman will store your requests/responses in the History List.

*   ✅ Useful to preview your previous Request/Response
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FNeDMfkGV3TDQoEwgOQp9%252FScreenshot%25202025-08-25%2520at%252014.02.04.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96cba38c-b30a-4380-a652-9d098c970e04&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ba2a14a3&sv=2)

Request History in the Compose View

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose#id-6.-settings)

6\. Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **SettingsRequest Timeout**: In Setting -> Tools Tab -> Request Timeout: Define a second that the Request will timeout. Use 0 to disable it. Available on Proxyman 4.13.0 or later

# Edit & Repeat | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/edit-and-repeat#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Edit & Repeat is a handy tool for developers who need to test the Endpoint directly on Proxyman app without making a new request from your browser or client app.

*   Rapidly change a **Query**, **Header**, **Body** of the selected request and test the Response from the server
    
*   Easily reproduce the bug from the server with a different set of params.
    
*   Support Form and JSON format.
    
*   Edit by Raw Message
    
*   Review Response data on the Right Panel (Proxyman 3.6.0+).
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FCJ7eudk5oBzFBiZffNH6%252F174536780-6ced0dc3-df59-4c51-a1a5-dc72cb30140f.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc7d254ae-e7a1-46b9-9f90-1ccce881dfb0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a94bd758&sv=2)

Edit and repeat the request

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/edit-and-repeat#id-2.-how-to-use-it)

2\. How to use it?

1.  Simply select your request -> Right Click -> Edit & Repeat
    
2.  The request data (Header, URL, Query, Body) is preserved and it's ready to edit
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FBYdQcLz5fSHrjyfVhol8%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202022-06-23%2520at%252014.58.23.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04eeb323-0b26-49b6-b42c-d9266c1c8616&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ebee730e&sv=2)

Edit and repeat on the selected request

[PreviousRepeat](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/repeat)
[NextCompose new Request](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose)

# JSONPath | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

JSONPath is a tool for quickly filtering from JSON data.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MfztiHjdwktchVUVdx7%252F-MfzurR3JU5X5vLm0O6T%252FScreen_Shot_2021-08-01_at_10_29_35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc2bb9669-14b1-417e-abd9-8ab4d112f8a3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=512bad43&sv=2)

Filter JSON data

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths#operator)

Operator

Operator

Description

`$`

The root element to query. This starts all path expressions.

`@`

The current node is being processed by a filter predicate.

`*`

Wildcard. Available anywhere a name or numeric are required.

`..`

Deep scan. Available anywhere a name is required.

`.<name>`

Dot-notated child

`['<name>' (, '<name>')]`

Bracket-notated child or children

`[<number> (, <number>)]`

Array index or indexes

`[start:end]`

Array slice operator

`[?(<expression>)]`

Filter expression. The expression must evaluate to a boolean value.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths#filter-operators)

Filter Operators

Filters are logical expressions used to filter arrays. A typical filter would be `[?(@.age > 18)]` where `@` represents the current item being processed.

Operator

Description

\==

left is equal to the right (note that 1 is not equal to '1')

!=

left is not equal to the right

<

left is less than right

<=

left is less or equal to the right

\>

left is greater than right

\>=

left is greater than or equal to the right

\=~

left matches regular expression \[?(@.name =~ /foo.\*?/i)\]

in

left exists in right \[?(@.size in \['S', 'M'\])\]

nin

left does not exists in right

subsetof

left is a subset of right \[?(@.sizes subsetof \['S', 'M', 'L'\])\]

anyof

left has an intersection with right \[?(@.sizes anyof \['M', 'L'\])\]

noneof

left has no intersection with right \[?(@.sizes noneof \['M', 'L'\])\]

size

size of left (array or string) should match right

empty

left (array or string) should be empty

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths#path-examples)

Path Examples

Given the JSON Data.

JsonPath

Result

$.store.book\[\*\].author

The authors of all books

$..author

All authors

$.store.\*

All things, both books and bicycles

$.store..price

The price of everything

$..book\[2\]

The third book

$..book\[-2\]

The second to last book

$..book\[0,1\]

The first two books

$..book\[:2\]

All books from index 0 (inclusive) until index 2 (exclusive)

$..book\[1:2\]

All books from index 1 (inclusive) until index 2 (exclusive)

$..book\[-2:\]

Last two books

$..book\[2:\]

Book number two from tail

$..book\[?(@.isbn)\]

All books with an ISBN number

$.store.book\[?(@.price < 10)\]

All books in store cheaper than 10

$..book\[?(@.price <= $\['expensive'\])\]

All books in store that are not "expensive"

$..book\[?(@.author =~ /.\*REES/i)\]

All books matching regex (ignore case)

$..\*

Give me everything

$..book.length()

The number of books

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jsonpaths#reference)

Reference

*   [https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath](https://github.com/json-path/JsonPath)
    

[PreviousMultipart Form-Data Previewer](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/multipart-form-data-previewer)
[NextJQ](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/jq)

Last updated 4 years ago

# Breakpoint Templates | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 3.1.0+, you can create a Breakpoint Template for Requests and Response that allows developers to reuse it.

*   Create new Template for Request: HTTP Method, URL, Headers
    
*   Template for Response: Status Code, Headers
    
*   Boots productivity when using the [Breakpoint tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint#1.-whats-it)
    .
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F0whNSLK2NsklQTWsoKgY%252F153364144-b1a8378e-dff8-412b-a3b6-4bfad44f9d61.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd8d7061a-b1d7-472f-a583-d664670ccdfb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8ff077a2&sv=2)

Breakpoint Template for Request/Response

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates#id-2.-how-to-create-a-new-template)

2\. How to create a new template?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates#create-a-new-one)

Create a new one

1.  Tools Menu -> Breakpoint -> Breakpoint Template
    
2.  CMD+N or SHIFT+CMD+N to create a template for Request/Response
    
3.  Defind your Request/Response template
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates#use-the-existing-one)

Use the existing one

1.  Create a Breakpoint Rule -> Make sure your request/response -> Make sure it hits the Breakpoint
    
2.  Click Raw Tab -> Template button -> Request/Response -> Create new request/response
    
3.  Done
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint-templates#id-3.-how-to-use-it)

3\. How to use it?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  When a request/response hit a Breakpoint -> Click Raw Tab
    
2.  Template -> Request/Response -> Select your template
    
3.  It will replace the current data with the template one.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FtLPPOneBdYRR0Y7WiUu8%252F153364160-7fde3bdb-2941-4cd1-a62f-77a4a4ba7013.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8ad4ece0-826f-4fc7-9718-50400fe74fb8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=96e70fda&sv=2)

Use Breakpoint Template

# No Caching | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Prevent the server or client from caching your Request or Response, and you always get the latest change from the server.

No Caching tools will affect all HTTP Request and Response, which enabled SSL Proxying.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching#id-2.-whats-for)

2\. What's for?

*   If you would like to **see the latest HTTP Response changes** from the Server or Client and ignore all caching layers
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching#id-3.-how-it-works)

3\. How it works

No Caching tool will manipulate all requests by adding or removing caching HTTP Headers, which are described in the following table.

HTTP Message

Remove

Add

Request

**If-Modified-Since** and **If-None-Match**

**Pragma: no-cache** and **Cache-control: no-cache**

Response

**Expires**, **Last-Modified,** and **ETag**

**Expires: 0** and **Cache-Control: no-cache**

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching#id-4.-how-to-use)

4\. How to use

*   Enable in **Tool Menu -> No Caching**
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5kUoPHDivENZr4LN56%252F-M5kVwl9fEys53qNNwEW%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252015.45.37.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D30790a7b-e5de-48f2-a361-ea7c272b44f6&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26a1eff5&sv=2)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5kUoPHDivENZr4LN56%252F-M5kWUcDLjQdfVToZaRN%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252015.48.05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D720528e0-e89c-4413-aae2-0d89c8cb26aa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=db04fafe&sv=2)

No Caching Status on the bottom right of Proxyman app

**⌥⌘N:** Toggl the No Caching Tool.

[PreviousCompose new Request](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/compose)
[NextBreakpoint](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/breakpoint)

# Block List | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/blacklist#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Block List Tool is useful when you would like to **block or hide** certain domains during a debugging session.

For instance, you can use Block List in the following situations:

*   Block all ads requests from particular domains
    
*   Block all analytic requests that flood the working space
    
*   Block all annoying ping requests from your app to reduce the number of requests that appear on Proxyman
    
*   Hide analytic traffic from your website without blocking it.
    

All blocked domains in the Block List will **drop the connection.**

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252Fh7eV4gZC8FosDZOIFr5Y%252FScreenshot%25202025-09-05%2520at%252021.11.17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58bf6a8c-d987-4733-94d1-2055be45f661&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b1df0364&sv=2)

Block certain Requests by Domains or Client

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/blacklist#id-2.-block-actions)

2\. Block Actions


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Block List supports some block actions that can suit your needs:

Block Action

Description

Block & Hide Request

Matched requests are blocked and don't display on the app.

Block & Display

Matched requests are blocked, but display the blocked requests on the app.

Hide, but not Block

Just hiding the matched requests without blocking them. It's useful if you'd hide your annoying requests but don't block them.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FwAI9lqgKzSx39SC4HIS0%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202022-01-10%2520at%252014.43.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd82dbf86-bfac-406f-b3b3-2c605599f8e9&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4581e83e&sv=2)

Create a Block / Hide Rule

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/blacklist#id-3.-how-to-use-it)

3\. How to use it?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Tools** Menu -> **Block List**
    
*   Right-click on the requests or domains -> **Tools** -> **Block List...**
    

**⌥⌘\[** to quick open Block List Window\
\
[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/blacklist#id-4.-block-all-traffic-from-a-given-app)\
\

\

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\

    \
