# async/await Request | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman macOS v3.5.0 and Windows/Linux v2.11.0 or later, you can use `async / await` to make an HTTP/HTTPS call for retrieving external resources inside your Script.

*   On macOS: Use \`$http\`
    
*   On Windows/Linux: Use built-in \`axios\`
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#sample-post-request-with-json-body-macos)

Sample: POST Request with JSON Body (macOS)

Copy

    async function onResponse(context, url, request, response) {  
      // Define JSON Body and Header
      // Make sure "Content-Type" is "application/json"
      var param = {
        body: {
          "user": {
            "name": "Proxyman"
          }
        },
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
      }
    
      // POST request with await
      var output = await $http.post("https://httpbin.org/post", param);
      
      // Get Status Code
      console.log(output.statusCode);
      
      // Get body
      console.log(output.body)
      
      // Get header
      console.log(output.headers)
      
      // Done
      return response;
    }

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-2.-how-to-use-on-macos)

2\. How to use on macOS?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#method)

Method

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#output-format)

Output format

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#sample-code)

Sample Code

*   [GET Request with Query](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#get-request-with-query)
    
*   [POST Request with JSON Body](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#post-request-with-json-body)
    
*   [POST Request with application/x-www-form-urlencoded body](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#post-request-with-application-x-www-form-urlencoded-body)
    
*   [PUT / PATCH / DELETE Request](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#put-patch-delete-request)
    

Please checkout the [HTTP Snippet code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#make-async-await-http-request)
 for more sample code.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-3.-how-to-use-on-windows-linux)

3\. How to use on Windows/Linux?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman Windows/Linux ships with a built-in [axios](https://github.com/axios/axios)
 library, it means we can use the axios syntax to make HTTP(s) requests.

For example:

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-4.-notes)

4\. Notes


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Make sure you defined the **async** function on `onRequest()` and `onResponse()`:
    

*   Request Timeout is 10 seconds.
    
*   The inline HTTP Request doesn't go through the Proxyman Proxy, so it isn't affected by other debugging tools.
    
*   Use can use `await $http.get()` on both `onRequest()` and `onResponse()`
    
*   Make sure the Body type is matched with the Content-Type header.
    

**JSON Body with application/json**

**Encoded form Body with application/x-www-form-urlencoded**

[PreviousScripting](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script)
[NextAddons](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. How to use on macOS?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-2.-how-to-use-on-macos)
    
*   [3\. How to use on Windows/Linux?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-3.-how-to-use-on-windows-linux)
    
*   [4\. Notes](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request#id-4.-notes)
    

Copy

    var output = await $http.get("https://httpbin.org/anything");
    var output = await $http.post("https://httpbin.org/anything");
    var output = await $http.put("https://httpbin.org/anything");
    var output = await $http.update("https://httpbin.org/anything");
    var output = await $http.delete("https://httpbin.org/anything");

Copy

    var output = await $http.get("https://httpbin.org/anything");
    console.log(output)
    
    // print
    {
        "statusCode": <Int>,
        "headers": <Object>,
        "body": <Object>
    }

Copy

    async function getUser() {
      try {
        const response = await axios.get('/user?ID=12345');
        console.log(response);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(error);
      }
    }

Copy

    async function onRequest(context, url, request) {
        var output = await $http.get("https://httpbin.org/get");
        return request;
    }
    
    async function onResponse(context, url, request, response) {
        var output = await $http.get("https://httpbin.org/get");
        return response;
    }

Copy

    var param = {
        body: {
          "name": "Proxyman",
        },
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
      }

Copy

    var param = {
        body: {
          "key1": "value1",
          "key2": "value2"
        },
        headers: {
          "Content-Type": "application/x-www-form-urlencoded"
        }
      }

# I couldn't see any traffics on Proxyman | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-1.-problems)

1\. Problems

*   After launching the app, the request list is empty
    
*   There are no requests captured by Proxyman?
    
*   I don't see any requests on the app
    
*   I can see some request on my Mac, but no request on my remote devices (iOS, Android)
    

For remote devices (iOS or Android), please check out this [troubleshoot](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy)
.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5oNQOA8eEMdsDo1W4b%252F-M5oNlGIE51483XhMSa4%252FScreen_Shot_2020-04-26_at_09_48_10.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db8e3b7fc-181f-4b03-8d5e-6f2e33f14d7d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a985a8&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.-solution)

2\. Solution

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.1-turn-off-all-vpn-apps-on-your-mac-machine)

2.1 Turn OFF all VPN apps on your Mac machine

Some VPN apps accidentally revert the HTTP Proxy in Network as soon as Proxyman overrides it. As a result, HTTP Traffic won't go through Proxyman port at 9090.

Close all VPN app if possible and relaunch Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.2.-double-check-http-proxy-in-network)

2.2. Double-check HTTP Proxy in Network

Proxyman would override or revert the HTTP Proxy at the launch time or exit, but some apps could revert back.

Let open System Preference -> Network -> Wifi -> Proxies tab:

*   Check the **Web Proxy (HTTP)** and **Secure Web Proxy (HTTPS)**
    
*   Make sure the port is the same as the Proxyman port
    
*   IP is **127.0.0.1**
    

Save and check the requests on Proxyman

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5oNQOA8eEMdsDo1W4b%252F-M5oPPHJI6eMwhUjoubn%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-26%2520at%252009.54.53.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D83d8e206-5bfb-442e-a871-b2fea33fca35&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ac8e459f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.3-install-proxyman-helper-tool)

2.3 Install Proxyman Helper Tool

By default, Proxyman attempts to override the system HTTP Proxy by using `networksetup` CLI, but it might be failed in certain scenarios.

\=> Let's try to install Proxyman Helper Tool. This tool will override the system HTTP Proxy properly. Please open Proxyman Preference -> Advanced Tab -> Install Helper Tool

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MJPOMkRPevh8tQznx08%252F-MJPPWnJw44Jz-e57Mqi%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-12_at_08_24_05.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D31598950-209a-414d-b018-ae6a20a133d7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d85d7ce&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.4-some-http-https-requests-are-missing-from-proxyman)

2.4 Some HTTP/HTTPS Requests are missing from Proxyman

Alamofire or URLSession might use the cached response for your request. As a result, the actual request doesn't hit the server. Thus, Proxyman could not capture and display it on the app.

Solution:

*   Disable the cache mechanism on URLSession or Alamofre.
    
*   Use the [No Caching Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/no-caching)
     (⌥⌘N)
    

[Previous\*.local requests do not appear on Proxyman](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/.local-doesnt-appear-in-proxyman)
[NextI couldn't see any requests from 3rd-party network libraries](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-requests-from-3rd-party-network-libraries)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. Problems](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-1.-problems)
    
*   [2\. Solution](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.-solution)

*   [2.3 Install Proxyman Helper Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.3-install-proxyman-helper-tool)
    
*   [2.4 Some HTTP/HTTPS Requests are missing from Proxyman](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/i-couldnt-see-any-traffics-on-proxyman#id-2.4-some-http-https-requests-are-missing-from-proxyman)

# My Remote Devices (iOS/Android) could not connect to Proxyman? | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-1.-problems)

**1\.** Problems


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   ❌ My iOS or Android Devices could not access the Internet after changing the Proxy Config in the Wifi Setting.
    
*   ❌ I can't download the certificate from **http://cert.proxyman.io** or **http://proxy.man/ssl**
    

For Android, please follow the [second section](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#android-devices-and-android-emulator)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-2.-solution-ios-devices)

2\. Solution: iOS devices


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Please make sure to double-check the following steps:

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-0.-issue-with-ios-16-physical-devices-simulator)

0\. Issue with iOS 16 Physical Devices / Simulator

Some reports from Proxyman's users, that **Proxyman** and **Charles Proxy** could not capture any traffic from iOS 16 devices/simulator, even though they config the HTTP Proxy.

It's a bug from iOS, we have to wait for the Apple team to fix it.

To workaround:

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#ios-16-physical-devices)

iOS 16 physical devices:

*   Forget the network and try to connect again.
    
*   Use [Atlantis Framework](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis)
     to capture the traffic
    
*   Use iOS 15 devices
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#ios-16-simulator)

iOS 16 Simulator:

*   Use iOS 15 Simulators
    
*   Use [Atlantis Framework](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis)
     to capture the traffic.
    

[iOS 16 and iOS 17 issues](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-1.-make-sure-your-mac-device-and-ios-android-devices-are-on-the-same-network)

1\. Make sure your Mac device and iOS/Android devices are on the same network

If they're on a different network, they are unable to connect to each other.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-2.-make-sure-the-server-ip-and-port-number-must-match-with-proxyman)

2\. Make sure the server IP and Port number must match with Proxyman

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F5th87NuXdHcJVVHFHdT3%252FIMG_4110.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D563df522-8c6e-44ea-85f5-ebe098633432&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2e37a713&sv=2)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M23a4e4ytcd0Sr111ZH%252F-M23ea8TqvpuPstOPCt9%252FScreen_Shot_2020-03-10_at_20_37_01.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D78e6491f-feb7-44be-ade3-ea0991b9cb43&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=536475dc&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-3.-turn-off-all-vpn-apps-from-macos-and-ios-android-devices)

3\. Turn OFF all VPN apps from macOS and iOS/Android devices

By default, the VPN app will **force** all traffic through the VPN server instead of the Proxyman Proxy server (at 9090). Therefore, there are no requests that appear on the Proxyman app.

Turn OFF all VPN apps will fix it:

*   For **iOS** Devices: Navigate to Settings -> General -> VPN and make sure the VPN status is **OFF**
    
*   For **Android** Devices: Find the VPN setting on the Settings app and turn it OFF
    
*   For **macOS**: Quit all VPN apps
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-4.-firewall-settings-macos)

4\. Firewall settings (macOS)

By default, a Firewall might block all incoming traffic to your mac. Thus, your remote devices might not be able to connect to Proxyman.

On **macOS**: Navigate to **System Preference -> Security & Privacy -> Firewall tab -> Option**

**Verify that:**

*   Block All incoming connections is **OFF**
    
*   Proxyman app **allows incoming connection**
    
*   If there is no Proxyman app, please add the Proxyman app by clicking on + button
    
*   Automatically allow built-in software to receive incoming connection is **ON**
    
*   Automatically allowing downloaded signed software to receive incoming connections is **ON**
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M23a4e4ytcd0Sr111ZH%252F-M23gxs4aNNh1g_KORUo%252FScreen_Shot_2020-03-10_at_20_46_17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df0304fda-f1e0-4d28-b505-70ed4e16b52c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3af730f&sv=2)

Firewall setting on macOS

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-4.-firewall-setting-windows-10-11)

4\. Firewall Setting (Windows 10/11)

Windows 10/11 might block Proxyman, and iPhone/Android devices could not connect to the app. To fix it:

1.  Search and open the "Windows Defender Firewall" app -> Click the "Advanced Setting" on the left panel
    
2.  Select "Inbound Rules"
    
3.  Find Proxyman.exe -> Double-click to open the setting
    
4.  Select "Allow the Connection" in the General Tab
    
5.  Click OK
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FEMq0r5Sx15yeAwQLJa5x%252FCleanShot%25202023-01-05%2520at%252009.26.50%25402x.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f47290c-4c90-425f-8f40-4d643ac560ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d0ac319&sv=2)

Allow Proxyman on Windows Firewall

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-5.-if-youre-using-the-company-network-ask-the-security-team-to-open-proxymans-port-9090)

5\. If you're using the Company Network, ask the Security team to open Proxyman's port 9090

Some companies block certain ports by default. Therefore, your iOS devices couldn't access to Proxyman's port at 9090.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-6.-use-private-browser-on-safari-to-open-http-cert.proxyman.io-or-http-proxy.man-ssl)

6\. Use Private Browser on Safari to open http://cert.proxyman.io or http://proxy.man/ssl

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-7.-im-still-unable-to-connect)

7\. I'm still unable to connect.

If you follow all the above steps and all configuration is correct but it hasn't resolved your cases yet.

Please try to **ON/OFF your Wifi, Forget the Wifi Network (iOS),** and **Restart the Computer**.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-8.-still-does-not-work-ios-app-only)

8\. Still does not work? (iOS app only)

Manual Override the HTTP Proxy, install and trust Proxyman on iOS devices is hard. We understand that. Let's try Atlantis, which is an iOS framework that helps you do it automatically.

[Atlantis for iOS](https://docs.proxyman.com/atlantis/atlantis-for-ios)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#android-devices-and-android-emulators)

Android Devices and Android Emulators


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-1.-after-setting-http-proxy-in-wifi-setting-i-could-not-open-http-proxy.man-ssl)

1\. After setting HTTP Proxy in Wifi Setting, I could not open http://proxy.man/ssl

*   [Please follow the above troubleshooting](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#1-make-sure-your-mac-device-and-ios-devices-are-on-the-same-network)
     ☝️
    
*   Double-check the Wifi Connection in the Emulator. It must be Connected Status (not Limited Connection or No Internet)
    

If it happens, please try to **forget the network** and **re-connect the Wifi.**

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FrO7687XSKWXvTi4uD4nU%252FScreen_Shot_2020-09-29_at_8_52_45_PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63877cdb-74f4-4f5d-a380-1552ff500f32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9160f090&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-2.-install-and-trust-proxyman-ca-for-android-with-api-30)

2\. Install and trust Proxyman CA for Android with API 30+

From Android Emulator API 30+, it requires extra steps to trust the Proxyman Certificate

*   Open http://proxy.man/ssl from Google Chrome to download the certificate
    
*   Setting app -> Security -> Encryption & Credentials -> Install a Certificate -> CA Certificate -> Install Anyway and Select CA Proxyman Certificate in your storage
    

You can verify that by opening Trusted Credentials -> User Tab

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FAfAc1OhdtkcQHS530Leo%252FScreen_Shot_2020-09-29_at_9_00_46_PM.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a13c1bb-6f8d-4241-addc-bcd6fc14d3fa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=85d9ce4a&sv=2)

Trust the Certificate

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-3.-my-android-physical-devices-or-emulator-connection-is-not-stable)

3\. My Android Physical Devices or Emulator connection is not stable.

It probably dues to the Android devices/emulators, the only way might fix it is to change the DNS from your Mac or Android Device to **8.8.8.8**

*   **On macOS**: Open System Preference -> Network -> Select Wifi -> Advanced -> Select DNS Tab -> Enter **8.8.8.8** on DNS Server Table
    
*   **On Android Device**: Open Wifi Setting -> Set DNS as **8.8.8.8**
    

Read more at [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/636](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/636)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MJPNG3YAkmXqa3cpCQW%252F-MJPO1WnDIkVjR9DpjcV%252FScreen_Shot_2020-10-12_at_08_18_35.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fa7e2cf-cf49-4d1e-83ca-afa612f0fd99&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2801c26e&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-4.-the-adb-command-not-found-when-using-android-emulator-automatic-script)

4\. The `adb` command not FOUND! when using Android Emulator Automatic Script

If you attempt to override Android Emulator and get the following error:

Please install the `adb` command line then try again!

*   [How to install ADB](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator#4-how-does-it-work)
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/my-ios-devices-couldnt-connect-to-proxyman-via-proxy#id-5.-if-you-debug-with-android-emulator-and-could-not-know-how-to-install-and-trust-proxyman-certifica)

5\. If you debug with Android Emulator and could not know how to install and trust Proxyman Certificate, please consider using [Automatic Script for Android Emulator](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator)

[PreviousProxyman does not work with VPN apps](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/proxyman-does-not-work-with-vpn-apps)

# Built-in JS Libraries | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Proxyman provides certain useful bundled JS Libraries that help you achieve some tasks easily

Library Location: **~/Library/Application\\ Support/com.proxyman.NSProxy/addons/libs**

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-2.-built-in-libraries)

2\. Built-in Libraries

Name

Description

Source

base64.js

Contains basic Base64 Encode/Decode

\-

atob.js

window.atob()

[https://github.com/jsdom/abab](https://github.com/jsdom/abab)

btoa.js

window.btoa()

[https://github.com/jsdom/abab](https://github.com/jsdom/abab)

hashes.js

Contains various hashing function: MD5, RIPEMP-160, SHA1, SHA256, SHA512, HMAC

[https://github.com/h2non/jshashes](https://github.com/h2non/jshashes)

lodash.js

Contains various text transformed functions

[https://lodash.com](https://lodash.com/)

vkBeautify.js

pretty-print or minify text in XML, JSON, CSS and SQL formats.

[https://github.com/kayhadrin/vkBeautify/](https://github.com/kayhadrin/vkBeautify/)

crypto-js.min.js

JavaScript implementations of standard and secure cryptographic algorithms, e.g. DES, AES, Rabbit, ... (Version 3.3.0)

[https://cryptojs.gitbook.io/docs/](https://cryptojs.gitbook.io/docs/)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-3.-how-to-import-my-own-js-library)

3\. How to import my own JS Library?

1.  You can provide your own JS Library, but make sure you bundle all dependencies by using [Browserify](http://browserify.org/)
     or [WebPack](https://webpack.js.org/)
     to a single JS file.
    
2.  Make sure you export the func properly.
    
3.  Put the file at **~/Library/Application\\ Support/com.proxyman.NSProxy/addons/libs/your-lib.js**
    
4.  Importing the file by using
    

For instance,

You might check built-in libraries for reference at **~/Library/Application\\ Support/com.proxyman.NSProxy/addons/libs/**

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-4.-notes)

4\. Notes

Thanks to [Ivan Mathy](https://github.com/IvanMathy)
 for creating Boop app that facilitates Proxyman's built-in add-ons.

[PreviousAddons](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons)
[NextWrite your own Addons](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/write-your-own-addons)

Last updated 4 years ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. Built-in Libraries](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-2.-built-in-libraries)
    
*   [3\. How to import my own JS Library?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-3.-how-to-import-my-own-js-library)
    
*   [4\. Notes](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries#id-4.-notes)
    

Copy

    require('@libs/your-lib.js');

Copy

    const Hashes = require('@libs/hashes.js');
    const { cssmin } = require('@libs/vkBeautify.js');
    const Lodash = require('@libs/lodash.js');
    const { atob } = require('@[email protected]')

# Access Control | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/access-control#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's an advanced feature, which allows you to define how Remote Devices (iPhone, Android, other computers) can connect to the Proxyman app. It's designed for enterprise users for better security.

Access via **Tools Menu** -> Proxy Setting -> Access Control.

Mode

Description

Allow All

All Remote Connections can connect to Proxyman (Default).

Disallow All

All Remote Connections are not allow to connect to Proxyman.

Specify Remote Device by IP

Define which device can connect to the Proxyman app.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FzJwU5MqOdh4icM3PxOlZ%252FScreenshot%25202023-01-23%2520at%252009.25.40.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6718f108-5c53-4922-aec4-0446bfcc624a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cec6473b&sv=2)

Access Control UI

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FTv31V8COAJB6hiKoBVZs%252FScreenshot%25202023-01-19%2520at%252014.31.47.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D82cfae97-6b48-4e72-ba18-855dfccf58b5&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=eaf207f1&sv=2)

Prompt to allow unauthorized connections

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/access-control#id-2.-override-the-access-control-mode-by-command-lines)

2\. Override the Access Control mode by Command Lines


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 4.4.0, it's possible to override the Access Control by the following CLI.

It's useful if your company would enforce the mode without using GUI.

[PreviousDiff](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/diff)
[NextDNS Spoofing](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/dns-spoofing)

Last updated 2 years ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/access-control#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. Override the Access Control mode by Command Lines](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/access-control#id-2.-override-the-access-control-mode-by-command-lines)
    

Copy

    $ defaults write ~/Library/Preferences/com.proxyman.NSProxy.plist accessControlModeString "allowAll"
    $ defaults write ~/Library/Preferences/com.proxyman.NSProxy.plist accessControlModeString "disallowAll"
    $ defaults write ~/Library/Preferences/com.proxyman.NSProxy.plist accessControlModeString "specificIP"

---

# SSL Error from HTTPS Request/Response | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#id-1.-problems)

1\. Problems


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   You could not see any HTTPS traffic on the Proxyman app
    
*   You get SSL Error from HTTPS Requests and Responses.
    
*   You get **SSL Handshake Failed**
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5lO1HbZnnLbTXZtxBy%252F-M5lOSoKiG1qXJ0Tqh-L%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252019.52.38.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D81ddc918-1d2a-4023-a09a-0647858d65e0&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2a4d0963&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#id-2.-solution)

2\. Solution


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are many reasons why SSL Handshake Failed, please walk through the below steps to address the problem.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#id-2.1-mobile-devices)

2.1 Mobile devices


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#ios-device)

iOS Device

*   Follow this [iOS Setup Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-device)
     -> Make sure you've installed & trusted the Proxyman CA Certificate on your device.
    
*   If you're intercepting some popular apps (e.g. Facebook, Instagram, Apple, Whatsapp, ...): They are protected by SSL Pinning -> Impossible to intercept them.
    
*   Verify that your iOS app doesn't have SSL Pinning. If yes, please disable it.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#ios-simulator)

iOS Simulator

Follow this [iOS Simulator Setup Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator)
 -> Make sure you've installed & trusted the Proxyman CA Certificate on your device.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#android-device)

Android Device

*   Follow this [Android Device Setup Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device)
     -> Make sure you've installed & trusted the Proxyman CA Certificate on your device.
    
*   Verify that the 5th step is completed (by adding your domain to two files: **res/xml/network\_security\_config.xml** and **AndroidManifest.xml**)
    
*   If you're trying to intercept Android apps that you're not an owner -> It isn't possible to intercept -> ❌
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#android-emulator)

Android Emulator

*   Follow this [Android Emulator Setup Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/android-device/automatic-script-for-android-emulator)
     -> Make sure you've installed & trusted the Proxyman CA Certificate on your device.
    
*   Verify that the 5th step is completed (by adding your domain to two files: **res/xml/network\_security\_config.xml** and **AndroidManifest.xml**)
    
*   If you're trying to intercept Android apps that you're not an owner -> It isn't possible to intercept -> ❌
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#react-native-app)

React Native app

*   If your app is a React Native app, please follow the [React Native Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/react-native)
    .
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#flutter)

Flutter

*   Please follow [Flutter Setup Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/flutter)
    

If you've tried and verified all the above steps, but still get SSL Errors?

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#verify-that-youre-able-to-see-https-request-response-from-https-google.com-without-any-errors)

Verify that you're able to see HTTPS Request/Response from https://google.com without any errors

1.  Get your devices
    
2.  Open the Web Browser (Safari on iOS or Google Chrome on Android)
    
3.  Visit **https://google.com**
    
4.  Select "Enable SSL Proxying" on this domain on the Proxyman app for macOS
    
5.  Verify if you're able to see the HTTPS Response or not.
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#success)

✅ Success

1.  You're able to see https://google.com HTTPS Response, which means you set up the Certificate correctly -> It's good ✅
    
2.  The problem might be from your apps. Let's try again on your domains/apps -> If the SSL Error still happens, a high chance that this app is protected by the SSL Pinning.
    
3.  If you believe that it's not an SSL Pinning case, please open a ticket on [Github](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues)
     (Please mention what device, OS Version, app name, etc)
    

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#failed)

❌ Failed!

*   It seems Proxyman Certificate is not installed or trusted correctly in your devices. Please go back to the [2.1 Mobile Device](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#2.1-mobile-devices)
     section and follow it.
    
*   If you verify that everything is done, but the SSL Error still happens, please open a ticket on [Github](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues)
     (Please mention what device, OS Version, app name, etc)
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#id-2.2-macbook-or-windows-pc)

2.2 Macbook or Windows PC


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

I get SSL Errors from:

*   **Mac devices (Macbook, Mac Mini, Mac Studio)** -> Install & Trust the Certificate on your Macbook -> Follow [macOS Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/macos)
    
*   **Windows** \-> Install and trust the certificate on your Windows machine -> Follow [Windows guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-windows/install-certificate)
    
*   Java -> Follow [Java VM Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/java)
    
*   Firefox -> Follow [Firefox Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/firefox)
    
*   Python -> Follow [Python Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/python)
    
*   Ruby -> Follow [Ruby Guide](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ruby)
    

Some networking libraries (Ruby, NodeJS, Python, Golang) don't trust the self-signed certificate by default. We have to explicitly tell the library to trust the certificate.

\=> To fix it, please google **"<Your framework/library> self-signed certificate",** a found some answers on StackOverflow.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/get-ssl-error-from-https-request-and-response#id-2.3-ssl-pinning)

2.3 SSL-Pinning?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   You're still unable to see HTTPS Response on your app, it seems that your app is protected by [SSL-Pinning](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/HTTP_Public_Key_Pinning)
    , which prevents MitM apps from seeing the content. All popular apps (Facebook, Apple, Instagram, Messenger, etc.) have this feature.
    
*   Please temporarily **disable SSL-Pinning** and try again.
    

Read more about SSL-Pining: [https://www.raywenderlich.com/1484288-preventing-man-in-the-middle-attacks-in-ios-with-ssl-pinning](https://www.raywenderlich.com/1484288-preventing-man-in-the-middle-attacks-in-ios-with-ssl-pinning)

If you've tried everything but are not sure what is wrong? Please open a [Github ticket](https://docs.proxyman.com/)
.

Please also mention: Proxyman macOS/Windows, Proxyman version, your iOS/Android device, etc.

[PreviousiOS 16 and iOS 17 issues](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues)
[NextI could not see any requests from my localhost server](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server)

Last updated 1 year ago

# Map Remote | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Map Remote (**⌘⌥R**) would help the developer to change the HTTP Request's location to a new destination server, per the configured rules, so the HTTP Response is transparently served from your client.

Map Remote also supports mapping from HTTP to HTTPS and vice-versa

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MC_ByEFfDEzSzI1C7Zz%252F-MC_DZnVSPfddI4tnDir%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-07-19%2520at%252010.17.34.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df468fd18-608d-4841-9c4b-fa47236b4f24&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=abb8c04e&sv=2)

Map Remote Rules

Check out common [Map Remote Config](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#7.-common-usages)
 when mapping from HTTP <-> HTTPS.

From Proxyman 4.3.0: Map Remote supports Websocket and Secure Websocket.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-2.-benefits)

2\. Benefits


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Use Production Endpoints on your Development website on certain endpoints without changing the source code
    
*   Use Development Endpoints on your Production website
    
*   Change certain request's URLs to different destinations
    
*   Able to replace requests components, such as Protocol, Host, Port, Path, or Query on the fly
    

To boost your productivity, you can use the [Scripting feature](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#1-whats-it)
 that allows you to achieve the same result as Map Remote by writing simple Javascript Code

For instance, [Snippet code to change Production to Localhost server](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#change-request-destination-schema-host-port-path)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-3.-map-remote-with-graphql-requests)

3\. Map Remote with GraphQL Requests


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 2.27.0+, Map Remote can work with GraphQL Request by a specific QueryName. Please check out the following GraphQL Document.

[GraphQL](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-4.-using-scripting-as-map-remote)

4\. Using Scripting as Map Remote ✅


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you get difficult to set up a complicated Map Remote Rule, you might easily do it by using the [Scripting Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#1-whats-it)
.

Please check out [Map Remote Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#8-map-remote-with-scripting)
 to learn how to use Scripting to achieve the same result as Map Remote.

For instance, it's straightforward to do the following by Scripting:

*   Map v1 to v2 endpoints
    
*   Map Production to Localhost
    
*   Map Localhost to Production
    
*   ...
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-5.-matching-rule)

5\. Matching Rule


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman supports [Regular Expression](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/foundation/nsregularexpression#1965590)
 and Wildcard from the 2.3.0 version. [Check out here](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex)

We can define matching rules by using [Wildcard or Regular Expression](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/regex)
.

For matched requests, Proxyman attempts to:

*   Replace Protocol, Host, Port, Path, and Query if it available
    
*   If the component is empty, it won't change the matched request's component
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MC_ByEFfDEzSzI1C7Zz%252F-MC_GHgRHPy8AUEjilO4%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-07-19%2520at%252010.17.44.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc380ce78-9b3f-4ee8-be9e-6e6ee31d3e76&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d9e0640b&sv=2)

*   Leave the Text Field blank to keep it unchanged from the matched request
    
*   The wildcard is not allow
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#debugging)

Debugging

To determine what Map Remote matches your URL, you can open The Request -> Summary Tab:

1.  Select your request
    
2.  Summary Tab -> Debugging Tools
    
3.  Check the Map URL
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FTzEwgRO7nyDgIKosKmVt%252FCleanShot%25202023-02-15%2520at%252009.23.58%25402x.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debb58d8c-e24a-4871-8e07-aa86719a0407&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=3c8e4298&sv=2)

How to debug the Map Remote

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#preserve-host-header)

Preserve Host Header

By default, Proxyman attempts to override the Host Header to match with the new Host in Remote Map. It's crucial to successfully make a request.

If you would like to preserve the original Host Header, please check ON in the "Preserve Host Header" checkbox when creating a new entry. Proxyman will preserve the Host value.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-6.-how-to-use)

6\. How to use


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Right Click on selected Request -> Tools -> Map Remote: Proxyman will fill in the necessary data from the selected request
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5kcNLYKkRb4y_kT34H%252F-M5kcjUlp-pVHTWFPxse%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252016.18.59.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da017a353-ca92-46f3-be11-5e93ff3b9300&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=37a9fc1f&sv=2)

Create a Map Remote

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-7.-common-usages)

7\. Common Usages


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-7.1-map-localhost-http-to-production-https)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FR7NQOMFyCWhHRUfDeFF0%252FScreenshot%25202023-02-15%2520at%252009.34.02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db1494d3a-6ac6-4f67-bee9-625a51ca2f33&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=65193c8f&sv=2)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-7.3-map-certain-url-to-another-host)

7.3 Map certain URL to another host

*   Rule: **https://proxyman.io/v1/user** (for instance)
    
*   Select **Any** and **Wildcard**
    
*   **Un-Check Include all subpaths of this URL:** Un-check means it doesn't map other subpaths
    

**Map To:**

*   Protocol: **https**
    
*   Host: New Host (e.g staging.proxyman.io)
    
*   Port: **443** (your local port)
    
*   Leave Path and Query Empty
    

**Result:**

Original URL

To URL

https://proxyman.io

https://proxyman.io (does not map the rule)

https://proxyman.io/v2/setting

https://proxyman.io/v2/setting (does not map the rule)

https://proxyman.io/v1/user?id=123&name=proxyman

https://staging.proxyman.io/v1/user?id=123&name=proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#id-7.4-map-websocket-from-localhost-to-production)

# iOS 16 and iOS 17 issues | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#id-1.-problem)

1\. Problem

*   iOS 16 or iOS 17 physical devices could not set HTTP Proxy to Proxyman. Setting app -> Current Wifi -> Configure Proxy -> Manual Proxy.
    
*   Proxyman might not capture the traffic from iOS 16/17 devices.
    

\=> It's an Apple bug.

This issue happens with **Charles Proxy**, Wireshark, Fiddler Everywhere, and other Web Debugging Proxy apps too.

Some users report that it's fixed on iOS 16.3 and later ✅

iOS 17 might have the same problem. **Forget this Network** might fix it.

See [Section 4](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#4.-solution-for-ios-16.3-or-later)
 for details.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#id-2.-how-do-i-know-its-a-bug-from-apple-not-proxyman)

2\. How do I know it's a bug from Apple, not Proxyman?

*   You can test it by following below steps:
    

1.  Close all Proxyman app
    
2.  Get your iPhone (iOS 16 or later) -> Setting app -> Wifi -> Your Wifi -> Configure Proxy -> Manual Proxy
    
3.  Set any random IP, e.g. 192.168.3.111
    
4.  Set any random Port, e.g 9999
    
5.  Save
    
6.  Open Safari app -> Visit https://google.com
    
7.  Confirm that you can access the Internet.
    

Since the IP and Port is **invalid**, but you can access the Internet, it indicates that it's Apple's bug 🆘

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#id-3.-solution-for-ios-16.3-or-earlier)

3\. Solution for iOS 16.3 or earlier

*   Try to forget the Wi-Fi hotspot and restart the device might help.
    
*   Use [Atlantis Framework](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis)
     to inspect the network.
    
*   Try to use iOS 15 physical devices.
    
*   Try to use the iOS 16 **Simulator**
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#id-4.-solution-for-ios-16.3-ios-17-or-later)

4\. ✅ Solution for iOS 16.3, iOS 17 or later

1.  Setting App -> WiFi -> Your WiFi -> **Forget this Network.**
    
2.  Setting app -> Wifi -> Your Wifi -> Configure Proxy -> Manual Proxy -> Enter the IP & Port -> Save.
    
3.  Double-check the Configure Proxy Setting
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F77ll6iOxkgjRyUjkd94j%252FIMG_7734727B4024-1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D917edce1-b5d5-49f8-b5d7-1aa35e732915&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1d14cf26&sv=2)

1.  Make sure it's \`Manual\`, If it's OFF, try again and Save. Sometimes, the proxy setting is not saved.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/ios-16-devices-issues#id-4.-further-discussions)

4\. Further discussions

*   [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1293](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/1293)

# WebSocket | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman could capture WebSocket (WS) and Secure WebSocket (WSS) traffic and easily preview it.

*   Capture WS/WSS from iOS Physical devices and iOS Simulator (Required [Atlantis framework](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis)
    )
    
*   Capture WS/WSS from Web Browser and Mac applications.
    
*   Capture WS/WSS from Android Physical devices or Android Emulators.
    
*   Prettier WebSocket Message.
    
*   Filter All / Sent / Received messages.
    
*   See the content in JSON / Tree Preview / HEX format.
    
*   Customize Columns: Frame, Length, Data, Time, ...
    
*   Auto-decode Binary Message to JSON if possible
    
*   Open WebSocket messages by external Editors, such as Sublime, VSCode
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#id-2.-capture-ws-wss-from-ios)

2\. Capture WS/WSS from iOS


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If your iOS app is using **URLSessionWebSocketTask** or iOS WebSocket libraries, e.g. Starscream, SocketRocket, etc. Proxyman might not be able to capture WS/WSS traffic.

*   **Reason**: Apple's intention. **URLSessionWebSocketTask** doesn't respect the System HTTP Proxy. All WS/WSS traffic goes directly to the Internet. Thus, Proxyman or Charles Proxy can't capture it.
    
*   Example Ap: [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/websocket-example-ios-app](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/websocket-example-ios-app)
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#solution-1-recommended-for-ios-17-or-later)

✅ Solution 1 (Recommended for iOS 17 or later)

1.  Follow the Setup guide for your [iOS Devices](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-device)
     or [iOS Simulators](https://docs.proxyman.com/debug-devices/ios-simulator)
     (Make sure we installed and trusted the certificate on your device)
    
2.  Proxyman Setup: Tools > Proxy Settings > SOCKS Proxy settings -> Enable it (Take note of the port)
    
3.  On the main Proxyman app -> Take note of a current IP in the Proxyman Tools bar
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FdYPaZhjGUBzUgxu9Z6Xx%252Fproxyman_capture_websocket_4.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D74d8aab6-5b85-4fc9-a753-00d1844d9190&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2b8f0523&sv=2)

Get Proxyman current IP

1.  On your app: Configure a SOCK Proxy in your App, make sure this is only available for debug builds by implementing a switch or something, you might not want your release build with this configuration.
    

*   For NWConnection
    

*   For URLSession and URLSessionWebSocketTask
    

1.  Done ✅
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FMlP1FUS4JbXjhNvqO5g1%252FScreenshot%25202024-11-29%2520at%25201.17.23%25E2%2580%25AFPM.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4bf61f2-fe72-42f3-a1e6-9b5b1e2c1ac7&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4bcfeaa0&sv=2)

Capture Websocket from iOS with Proxyman

*   Credit to [**FranklinSamboni**](https://github.com/FranklinSamboni)
     **->** [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/586#issuecomment-2125082129](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/Proxyman/issues/586#issuecomment-2125082129)
    
*   Tutorial: [https://proxyman.io/posts/2019-10-18-WebSocket-Debugging](https://proxyman.io/posts/2019-10-18-WebSocket-Debugging)
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#solution-2)

✅ Solution 2

Use [Atlantis Framework](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis#features)
 (developed by Proxyman) to capture WS/WSS **URLSessionWebSocketTask** traffic from iOS.

Read more at [https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis](https://github.com/ProxymanApp/atlantis#wswss-traffic)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#id-3.-capture-websockets-from-your-web-browser-chrome-safari-etc)

3\. Capture WebSockets from your Web Browser (Chrome, Safari, etc)


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Proxyman can capture WS/WSS from a Web Browser out of the box. No need to configure anything.
    
*   How to use: Open Google Chrome -> Visit your website that makes a WS/WSS connection -> Open Proxyman -> Find your websocket domains -> On the Response Panel -> Click Enable SSL Proxying on these domains. Open your Browser, and reload your website -> Proxyman will capture and decrypt WS/WSS ✅
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#id-4.-capture-websocket-from-nodejs-golang-python-server)

4\. Capture Websocket from NodeJS, Golang, Python Server


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Proxyman can capture WS/WSS from your NodeJS, Golang, Python, and Ruby server.
    
*   How to use: Read [Automatic Setup](https://docs.proxyman.com/automatic-setup/automatic-setup)
     to start your server on this Terminal -> Make a WS/WSS connection -> Proxyman automatically captures and decyrpts it ✅
    

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/websocket#id-5.-map-websocket-from-localhost-less-than-greater-than-production)

5\. Map Websocket from Localhost <-> Production


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's possible to map the WebSocket Traffic from localhost <-> Production. Please check out the [Map Remote Tool.](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/map-remote#7.4-map-websocket-from-localhost-to-production)

[PreviousProtobuf](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/protobuf)
[NextClear Session](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/clear-session)

Copy

    let parameters = webSocketURL.scheme == "wss" ? NWParameters.tls : NWParameters.tcp
    
    let options = NWProtocolWebSocket.Options()
    options.autoReplyPing = true
    
    parameters.defaultProtocolStack.applicationProtocols.insert(options, at: 0)
    
    if #available(iOS 17.0, *) {
        let socksv5Proxy = NWEndpoint.hostPort(host: "x.x.x.x", port: 8889) //  Please x.x.x.x with a real Proxyman IP
        let config = ProxyConfiguration.init(socksv5Proxy: socksv5Proxy)
        let context = NWParameters.PrivacyContext(description: "my socksv5Proxy")
        context.proxyConfigurations = [config]
    
        parameters.setPrivacyContext(context)
    }
    
    let connection = NWConnection(to: .url(webSocketURL), using: parameters)
    connection.start(queue: .main)

Copy

    private lazy var urlSession: URLSession = {
        let config = URLSessionConfiguration.default
        if #available(iOS 17.0, *) {
            let socksv5Proxy = NWEndpoint.hostPort(host: "x.x.x.x", port: 8889) //  Please x.x.x.x with a real Proxyman IP
            let proxyConfig = ProxyConfiguration.init(socksv5Proxy: socksv5Proxy)
            config.proxyConfigurations = [proxyConfig]
        }
    
        return URLSession(configuration: config, delegate: nil, delegateQueue: nil)
    }()

# GraphQL | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-1.-use-debugging-tools-with-graphql-requests)

1\. Use Debugging Tools with GraphQL Requests


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 2.27.0, we can use debugging tools with GraphQL Requests by specifying the GraphQL Query Name.

Matching by GraphQL QueryName works with Breakpoint, Map Local, Map Remote, Block List, Allow List, and the Scripting Tool.

#### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#how-to-use)

How to use

1.  Open the debugging tool (e.g. Breakpoint)
    
2.  Create new Rule
    
3.  Click on Use "Wildcard Dropdown" -> Advanced -> Check GraphQL QueryName.
    
4.  Enter the GraphQL QueryName
    

By doing this way, the debugging tool will match the original matching rule firstly, then match the GraphQL QueryName.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MacgPHEbYY2MrgWPuxX%252F-MacgUeszvheTmIlUrlG%252FScreen_Shot_2021-05-26_at_15_46_13.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0315198b-0784-4fb5-a749-3116495ed320&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26e376f1&sv=2)

Enable GraphQL QueryName

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MacgPHEbYY2MrgWPuxX%252F-MachGDOOk0ERFBap4p-%252FScreen_Shot_2021-05-26_at_15_48_17.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D513ed723-3395-40e0-b4b7-5c7109852545&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=4c933a6a&sv=2)

Specify the GraphQL QueryName

From build 3.0.0, Proxyman automatically fills the GraphQL Query Name when we create a debugging tool rule.

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-2.-graphql-prettier)

2\. GraphQL Prettier


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

From Proxyman 2.33.0, Proxyman can prettify/beautify GraphQL's Query Value. To do it, please open Tools Menu -> Custom Previewer Tab -> Check GraphQL checkbox.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MjJ69ff1vDV4wU6dKAD%252F-MjJ6Jbk2YKgmnqmYc6u%252FScreen_Shot_2021-09-11_at_15_58_08.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71007b3f-4f6c-44e8-a3b8-1e51393163bf&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=cdb1fb5&sv=2)

Beautify GraphQL Query

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-3.-show-graphql-query-name-on-the-main-table-view)

3\. Show GraphQL Query Name on the main table view


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

It's possible to extract and display the Query Name. Please Right-click on the Column Header and enable it.

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-MVepXPi2YNzkeoVqOWB%252F-MVetX1HGlYXY9NQS7A3%252FScreen_Shot_2021-03-13_at_16_20_42.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df7f16b9c-d200-4742-b158-db9f23cdd42b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9eb2898&sv=2)

Query Name from GrapQL Request

[Custom Header Column](https://docs.proxyman.com/basic-features/custom-header-column)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-4.-debug-graphql-requests-legacy-proxyman-2.26.0-and-below)

4\. Debug GraphQL Requests (Legacy - Proxyman 2.26.0 and below)


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

GraphQL uses the same URL to query different responses from the server, current debugging tools (e.g. Map Local, Breakpoint, Map Remote) doesn't work well.

However, by using the Scripting Tool, we can easily achieve:

*   Map Local for the response depends on QueryName
    
*   Manipulate the query, body, header for GraphQL Requests and Response
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#map-local-with-the-scripting-tool)

Map Local with the Scripting Tool

We can use the Scripting tool to map

1.  Open Proxyman
    
2.  Enable SSL Proxying on the GraphQL domain
    
3.  Verify that you can see HTTPS requests from your domain
    
4.  Right-Click on the flow -> Tool -> Scripting to create a script with the given URL
    
5.  To import a local file: Click the More button -> Import JSON or Other files -> Then selecting your file
    
6.  Use the following script shows you how to set a Local File to a GraphQL request with QueryName="user"
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#manipulate-headers-query-body)

Manipulate Headers, Query, Body

1.  Use the same code and change the queryName
    
2.  Please use [the snipped code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code#2-common-on-request-and-response)
     to change the values
    

[PreviousCustom Certificates](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/custom-certificates)
[NextNetwork Conditions](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/network-throttling)

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [1\. Use Debugging Tools with GraphQL Requests](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-1.-use-debugging-tools-with-graphql-requests)
    
*   [2\. GraphQL Prettier](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-2.-graphql-prettier)
    
*   [3\. Show GraphQL Query Name on the main table view](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-3.-show-graphql-query-name-on-the-main-table-view)
    
*   [4\. Debug GraphQL Requests (Legacy - Proxyman 2.26.0 and below)](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#id-4.-debug-graphql-requests-legacy-proxyman-2.26.0-and-below)
    
*   [Map Local with the Scripting Tool](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#map-local-with-the-scripting-tool)
    
*   [Manipulate Headers, Query, Body](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql#manipulate-headers-query-body)
    

Copy

    // Import file from More Button -> Import JSON or Other files 
    const file = require("@users/B02D96D5.default_message_32E64A5B.json");
    
    function onRequest(context, url, request) {
    
      // 1. Extract the queryName from the request
      var queryName = request.body.query.match(/\S+/gi)[1].split('(').shift();
      
      // Or extract the operationName
      var operationName = request.body.operationName
      
      // 2. Save to sharedState
      sharedState.queryName = queryName
      sharedState.operationName = operationName
      
      // Done
      return request;
    }
    
    function onResponse(context, url, request, response) {
    
      // 3. Check if it's the request we need to map
      if (sharedState.queryName == "user") {
        
        // 4. Import the local file by Action Button -> Import
        // Get the local JSON file and set it as a body (like Map Local)
        response.headers["Content-Type"] = "application/json";
        response.body = file;
      }
    
      // Done
      return response;
    }

# I could not see any requests from my localhost server | Proxyman

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#id-1.-problem)

1\. Problem


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

I develop a local NodeJS, Ruby, or Python Backend at **http://localhost:3000**, but when I visit **http://localhost:3000** from Google Chrome or Safari, there is no traffic on the Proxyman app.

**Why does this happen?** By default, on macOS, all localhost requests don't go through the System HTTP Proxy. Therefore, there is no traffic recorded by the Proxyman app.

![Proxyman can not capture any http localhost traffic](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FoMIYOFiGojtc8gDuKPhQ%252Fcapture_http_localhost_chrome_2.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20ccba33-5a02-412d-b50d-0683ae1865bb&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b2ff0390&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#id-2.-solution)

2\. Solution


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#id-2.1-new-solution-for-v6.3.0)

2.1 ✅ New Solution for v6.3.0

From Proxyman macOS v6.3.0, Proxyman can:

*   Capture `http://locahost:3000` or any localhost traffic in Google Chrome / Firefox without modifying the /etc/host file
    
*   Works with a single click
    
*   Tutorial: [https://proxyman.com/posts/how-to-capture-http-localhost-traffic-from-google-chrome](https://proxyman.com/posts/how-to-capture-http-localhost-traffic-from-google-chrome)
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#how-to-do-it)

How to do it

1.  In Proxyman app -> Go to the Setup Menu -> Automatic Setup -> Click on the "Google Chrome" button
    
2.  New Google Chrome will appear
    
3.  Done. Visit http://localhost:3000 and Proxyman can capture it
    

![capture HTTPS traffic from Google Chrome with Proxyman](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252F202Ww1pkI0lKkmSwkzgh%252Fcapture_http_localhost_chrome_1.jpeg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dab79aa40-2b97-401d-8475-a30467d93fea&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=95058449&sv=2)

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#id-2.2-old-solution)

2.2 Old solution


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

There are two solutions to fix it: You should follow either one of the following solutions.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#solution-1-map-localhost-to-the-domain-name-in-etc-hosts)

Solution 1: Map **localhost** to the domain name in `/etc/hosts`

1.  Open `etc/hosts` file with Vim or VS Code.
    

2\. Add Domain Name with both **IPv4** and **IPv6** (You can change the `proxyman.debug` with your name)

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FYl0L3IBWwwG0MXIHxK6i%252FScreenshot%25202023-09-01%2520at%252022.11.30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6c5c1ae-0cc7-42fc-9f05-49c090f4fbb4&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a478ce44&sv=2)

Add proxyman.debug in /etc/host

3\. Save the file with `sudo` permission

4\. Access your localhost server by **http://proxyman.debug:3000** (replace 3000 with your localhost ports)

6\. Enjoy debugging!

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-M5khYgr9Ma-4XAPDv1_%252F-M5kkqMh_FCLKY6nHCUw%252FScreen%2520Shot%25202020-04-25%2520at%252016.55.18.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4ccc7500-8491-421b-be95-a4e74c10059d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=76aec821&sv=2)

If you use a `local` as a suffix, e.g. proxyman.local, make sure to remove the \`\*.local\` from the Bypass Proxy List ([Instruction](https://docs.proxyman.io/troubleshooting/.local-doesnt-appear-in-proxyman#2-solution)
).

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/troubleshooting/couldnt-see-any-request-from-localhost-server#solution-2-use-localhost.proxyman.io-instead-of-localhost)

Solution 2: Use **localhost.proxyman.io** instead of **localhost**

Proxyman uses Cloudflare and sets the DNS of **localhost.proxyman.io** to 127.0.0.1 (localhost). As a result, Proxyman can capture the local traffic as usual ✅

For example:

Old URL

New URL

localhost:3000

localhost.proxyman.io:3000

localhost:8080

localhost.proxyman.io:8080

...

...

# Addons | Proxyman

1\. What's it?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Proxyman provides a list of handy built-in add-ons that help you to do many common tasks, such as MD5, SHA1 Hashing, Base64 Encode/Decode, Beautify XML, JSON, ....

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons#id-2.-built-in-addons)

2\. Built-in Addons

You can find sample code for all addons at [Addons Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code)

Description

3\. How to use addons?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Each addon will export the function that you can import by using the `require` function

To illustrate, Base64.js addon looks like:

Then, you can use it in the script:

You can find all addons code at **~/Library/Application\\ Support/com.proxyman.NSProxy/addons**

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons#id-4.-notes)

4\. Notes


-------------------------------------------------------------------------

The `require` function is not a built-in function from [JavascriptCore framework](https://developer.apple.com/documentation/javascriptcore)
, it's a custom function that Proxyman provides to allows the user to import the addons/libs easily.

Thanks to [Ivan Mathy](https://github.com/IvanMathy)
 for creating Boop app that facilitates Proxyman's built-in add-ons.

Addons folder will be overridden for every new Proxyman Update. Make sure you don't edit the addon. If need to modify, please copy to the **users** folder

[Previousasync/await Request](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request)
[NextBuilt-in JS Libraries](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries)

Last updated 4 years ago

*   [1\. What's it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons#id-1.-whats-it)
    
*   [2\. Built-in Addons](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons#id-2.-built-in-addons)
    
*   [3\. How to use addons?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons#id-3.-how-to-use-addons)

Copy

    // Base64.js
    const Base64 = require('@libs/base64.js');
    const { atob } = require("@libs/atob.js");
    const { btoa } = require("@libs/btoa.js");
    
    // atob / btoa
    // They're equivalent with window.atob and window.btoa
    
    exports.atob = atob;
    exports.btoa = btoa;
    
    // Basic Base64
    exports.base64Decode = (input) => {
        return Base64.decode(input)
    };
    
    exports.base64Encode = (input) => {
        return Base64.encode(input);
    };

Copy

    const { atob, btoa } = require("@addons/Base64.js")
    
    function onRequest(context, url, request) {
    
        // Encode base64 by using the export function
        var text = btoa("Hello World");
        
        console.log(text)
        // => SGVsbG8gV29ybGQ=
    }

# Scripting | Proxyman

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-1.-whats-it)

1\. What's it?

Proxyman offers a scripting feature that the developer could write the JS code to manipulate the Request/Response in a flexible way.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-2.-benefits)

2\. Benefits

*   Implement Map Local / Map Remote / Breakpoint by JS Code. **100x Faster**
    
*   Change the **Request Content**, including Domain, Host, Scheme, Port, Path, HTTP Method, HTTP Headers, Query, Body (Encoded-Form, JSON, plain-text)
    
*   Change the **Response Content**, including HTTP Status Code, HTTP Headers, and Body (JSON, Encoded-Form, plain-text, binary...)
    
*   Provide plenty of built-in addons and libraries for common tasks, such as Hashing, Encode/Decode, JSON-Text transformer, Beautify,...
    
*   Able to **write your own JS Addons or Libraries**
    
*   Designed to replace Rewrite GUI Tool from Charles Proxy
    
*   Assign and receive shared States between each script or current session with [ShareState or Environment Variables](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/environment-variables)
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252Fuploads%252FVb8s7zn5QOh5E3mH7USO%252FScreenshot%25202024-01-07%2520at%252014.52.47.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D944dfb39-f5ae-4cbd-9db8-4d313fe7c743&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1f4e8bc9&sv=2)

Scripting Tool

[Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-3.-how-to-use-it)

3\. How to use it?

You can access the Scripting Tool by:

*   Script Menu -> Script List (⌥⌘I)
    
*   Open Menu Context from Right Click on the Flow -> Tools -> Scripting
    

Please check out the [Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code)
 to see a collection of snippet JS codes for the Scripting Tool.

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-4.-scripting-with-graphql-requests)

4\. Scripting with GraphQL Requests

From Proxyman 2.27.0+, the Scripting Tool can work with a GraphQL Request by a specific QueryName. Please check out the following GraphQL Document.

[GraphQL](https://docs.proxyman.com/advanced-features/graphql)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-4.1-scripting-with-websocket)

4.1 Scripting with Websocket

From Proxyman v6.2.0 or later, it's possible to use the Script to

*   Modify the Websocket Request URL & Header
    
*   Modify the Websocket Response Headers
    
*   ❌ Can not modify the websocket message. Only URL and Headers are supported.
    
*   Refer to this snippet code.
    

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-5.-examples)

5\. Examples

The following guide will show you how to write JS code to change the Request domain from Production to Localhost and change the Response Body

1.  Make sure you enable SSL for this domain before creating the script.
    
2.  Open the Scripting Tool and create a new Script Entry (⌘N). You can right-click on the Request -> Tools -> Scripting => Proxyman will create a Script too
    
3.  Give the name and define a Matching Rule.
    
4.  Ex: **Name**\=Test on Localhost endpoint, **URL**\=https://proxyman.io
    
5.  Enable Run Script on **Request** and **Response** **checkbox**
    
6.  Start writing JS code for `onRequest` function
    

**onRequest(context, url, request) {}**

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#onrequest-object-format)

onRequest() Object Format

`context`, `url` and `request` Objects are defined by:

You can change any value of the request obj except `rawBody`

If the **body** variable is invalid format due to incorrect Content-Type in the Header. Please consider using the **rawBody** and manually parse the string.

The type of `request.body` replies on the Content-Type Header.

Content-Type Header

request.body

application/json or JSON families

Javascript Object

application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Javascript Object

plain-text or text-based Content-Type, Ex: application/js, text/css, text/html, ...

String

The rest: Binary Data (application/zip, application/octet-stream)

Uint8Array

Check out common JS code from Snipped Code Page

[Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code)

7\. Start writing code on `onResponse` function

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#onresponse-objects-format)

onResponse() Objects Format

`context`, `url`, `request`, and `response` objects are defined by:

You can change `statusCode`, `headers` and `body` from the response Obj

If the **body** variable is invalid format due to incorrect Content-Type in the Header. Please consider using **rawBody** and manually parse the string.

The type of `response.body` replies on the Content-Type Header

Content-Type Header

request.body

application/json or JSON families

Javascript Object

application/x-www-form-urlencoded

Javascript Object

plain-text or text-based Content-Type, Ex: application/js, text/css, text/html, ...

String

The rest (application/zip, application/octet-stream)

Uint8Array

You must return `request` and `response` object in `onRequest` and `onResponse` function

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-6.-built-in-addons-and-libraries)

6\. Built-in Addons and Libraries

Proxyman provides plenty of addons and libraries that help you achieve common tasks: Hashing, Encode/Decode, ...

[Addons](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/addons)
[Built-in JS Libraries](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/built-in-js-libraries)
[Snippet Code](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/snippet-code)

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-7.-debugging-js-error)

7\. Debugging JS Error

On certain occasions, you might encounter Javascript errors due to syntax errors, invalid code, ... You can debug by looking at error messages on the console or using `console.log().`

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-8.-use-scripting-as-a-mock-api)

8\. Use Scripting as a Mock API

From Proxyman 2.32.0, we can use the Scripting Tool as a Mock API. It means your request would never hit the server, and you have to define a Response Body. This behavior is the same with Map Local.

This feature is useful when the actual Restful API is not available yet. You can define and test it locally.

To enable the Mock API:

1.  Open the Scripting Tool -> Select the Script
    
2.  Enable Run as Mock API checkbox.
    

![](https://docs.proxyman.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1856518738-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-legacy-files%2Fo%2Fassets%252F-LlPt_6BePnJ3oK3saP1%252F-Mjmmr-T8SfIzLTD4zSD%252F-MjmnK40Iy1mMdQaU3mL%252FScreen_Shot_2021-09-17_at_14_59_30.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e35265f-1a40-4578-9178-ca40c4eb5143&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=7a9c4485&sv=2)

Enable Mock API

Then you can define a Response as usual:

### 

[](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-9.-notes)

9\. Notes

*   You must return `request` and `response` Object in `onRequest` and `onResponse` function.
    
*   **Proxyman 4.16.0 or later**: Proxyman now converts the Binary Data to **Uint8Array**
    
*   Proxyman 4.15.0 or earlier: Since Javascript doesn't have the Data object type, the Data Body will convert to **Base64 Encoded String** in Javascript. To pass Uint8Array, blob, or ArrayBuffer to the body, make sure you convert to **Base64 Encoded String.**
    

[PreviousWSL](https://docs.proxyman.com/proxyman-windows/wsl)
[Nextasync/await Request](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/async-await-request)

Last updated 1 month ago

*   [2\. Benefits](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-2.-benefits)
    
*   [3\. How to use it?](https://docs.proxyman.com/scripting/script#id-3.-how-to-use-it)
